Henderson Describes Difficult Points 41

(Geneva) The main leaders of the Disarmament Conference met at 4:20 this afternoon. Chairman Henderson briefly described the recent disarmament talks, saying that the talks should continue for several days because there is a need for political resolutions. There are still 14 unresolved issues, the most important of which are the three items of the trial period, punishment, and the implementation of the principle of equality. Henderson advocated the establishment of a permanent disarmament committee without waiting for all countries to ratify it, and said that twenty-four ratifications would be sufficient. After a brief discussion by the meeting, the meeting was adjourned until Saturday so that French Foreign Minister Poncet could return to Paris to participate in the House of Representatives meeting. It is heard that the General Committee of the Disarmament Conference will be convened on October 16. Japan was represented by Ambassador Sato to Belgium at today's leading group meeting. Before the meeting, US Chief Representative Davis expressed optimism, saying that everyone knows that things are already very bad, and something must be done. (Dispatch from Reuters on the 9th)

Wakatsuki Advocates for Naval Convention; US-Japan Naval Competition Would Greatly Harm Japan 42

(Tokyo) Wakatsuki, the chief representative of Japan at the 1930 London Naval Conference and the president of the Minseito Party, has been silent for two years. This afternoon, at the Minseito Party congress in Nagoya, he advocated for the naval convention and warned the audience that if the 1935 naval conference fails and ends, it will inevitably promote a new arms race between Japan and the United States, and Japan is afraid that it will suffer greatly. Wakatsuki also said that although the convention is not perfect, Japan's acceptance of it is of great benefit to the empire. Wakatsuki's speech is very relevant because it is the first response to the criticism of the naval convention made by the defendants in the assassination of Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi in the military court. (Dispatch from Reuters on the 11th)

(Geneva) The chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, reported on his travels to major European countries at a meeting of the chief committee, saying that the conclusion he reached on this trip was that all countries wanted an early decision. The British draft should be read a second time, so as to reach an agreement on the reduction and restriction of armaments. The situation is now fully clear. The difficulties hindering the general agreement can be divided into two categories: one is easier to solve, and the other is more difficult to handle. The first category is (1) non-use of force, (2) definition of aggressor, (3) overall terms and monitoring, (4) separate management of budget events, (5) bombing of the sky, (6) establishment of a permanent disarmament committee, (8) naval issues. The above are easier to solve. The second category is (1) the length of the first phase period stipulated in the convention, (2) the size of tanks and artillery positions, (3) how to reduce land warfare equipment, whether by destruction or other methods, (4) private manufacturing and sale of ammunition, (5) naval and army aviation, (6) penalties for violators. The above are more difficult to handle. As for the effective period of the convention, most countries advocate for five years, and some advocate for eight years, which is divided into two phases, the first four years being a trial period. The permanent disarmament committee can be responsible for determining whether the control and monitoring agencies are effective during the trial period. It is his intention that the convention does not have to be ratified before the permanent committee opens. German representative Nadolny hopes that the General Assembly will read the British draft a second time, and British representative Eden is responsible for drafting the points in the draft that have already been agreed upon by the representatives. (Dispatch from Reuters on the 9th)

Six Central and South American Countries Sign Anti-War Treaty; Aggression Deemed an Outlaw Act; Bolivia and Peru Not Participating 43

Reuters, Brazilian capital, 10th. Today, representatives from six countries—Argentina, Brazil, Chile, Mexico, Paraguay, and Uruguay—signed an anti-war treaty here, deeming aggression and seizure of land to be outlaw acts. Many diplomats and important figures were present to witness the signing ceremony. It is noteworthy that Bolivia did not join the treaty. Although Peru agrees to the treaty in principle, it wants to wait for the results of the Pan-American conference in Uruguay's capital before signing the treaty.

League of Nations Assembly Closes; Additional Seat for Council, Portugal Elected; High Commissioner Established to Handle Jewish Abuse Cases; Germany Votes Against Minority Issues 44

(Geneva) This morning, the League of Nations Assembly held its final meeting and passed the resolution on minority issues proposed by the French representative. (Note: The first part of this case stipulates that all countries should treat residents who are in a minority position due to race, religion, and language fairly and tolerantly in the spirit of the current treaties, the same as other residents, even for countries that have been relieved of all obligations by the League of Nations. The second part recognizes that excluding certain kinds of people hinders the rights of minorities and violates current treaties. (However, the German representative voted against the resolution because it involved Jews, rendering it invalid, but its moral power remains complete, because the League of Nations Assembly ignored Germany's opposition and voted in favor of the resolution as a whole, putting Germany in an isolated position. The Assembly then approved the decision on German refugee relief affairs, i.e., establishing a high commissioner to handle this matter, and other issues.) Finally, the chairman, the representative of South Africa, Watt, made the closing remarks as usual, describing the work of the General Assembly one by one. The General Assembly ended its work at 3:30 in the afternoon and announced its closure. (Dispatch from Havas on the 11th)

(Geneva) Portugal was elected today to fill the additional seat on the Council of the League of Nations. (Dispatch from Reuters on the 9th)

Public Telegram 71

Telegram from Ningbo: To the editors of the Shanghai Shen Bao: Greetings. The Tianyi Pavilion in Yin County was originally built by Fan Dongming, the Secretary of War during the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty, and his son Fan Shou. In addition to storing books, it was also extensively landscaped with gardens and pavilions for scholars to visit and relax. During the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, Fan Maozhu, an eighth-generation descendant of the Secretary of War, presented books for inspection and was rewarded with 10,000 volumes of the Complete Collection of Illustrations and Writings of Ancient and Modern Times. At that time, the Qing court discussed establishing Yuan Pavilions and other structures, and sent officials to Yin County to survey the style of the pavilions and order their imitation. The richness of the Tianyi Pavilion's collection and the refinement of its architecture are known to all, from our country to overseas nations. It has always been the premier collector. From the Ming Dynasty to the present, more than 400 years have passed. It has suffered from wars and looting, and most of the books have been damaged. The gardens have become overgrown with weeds. Among the descendants of Secretary of War Fan, there is no lack of intelligent people, but with a large population, it is difficult to reach a consensus. Moreover, the pavilion occupies a large area, and construction is not easy. For this reason, discussions about repairs are often interrupted. On September 18th and 19th of this year, a typhoon caused disaster, and the entire eastern wall of the pavilion collapsed. The wind and rain damaged the books. If repairs are not carried out quickly, the remaining texts and slips are in imminent danger. The committee held its fourth regular meeting on October 1st of this year. The matter was proposed by members Ma Lian, Chen Baolin, Ye Qianliang, and others. After discussion, the committee decided to

organize a committee to repair the Tianyi Pavilion, with preparatory members responsible for carrying out the work first. In addition to notifying the descendants of the Fan family to start emergency repairs, the cost of repairing the entire pavilion is considerable. It is proposed to solicit donations from domestic cultural institutions and scholars interested in archaeology, so that work can begin as soon as possible. If you are willing to help generously, please send the funds directly to the Yin County Literature Committee in Zhongshan Park, Ningbo, or through the Shanghai Ningbo Association or the Yin County government. The matter concerns national culture, and not only the people of Yin County and the descendants of the Fan family are deeply grateful. Furthermore, regarding the catalogue of the Tianyi Pavilion, Ruan Yuntai engraved a ten-volume catalogue during the Jiaqing period, Qian Zhuting compiled a one-volume epigraphic catalogue, and Xue Shuyun continued to engrave a six-volume catalogue of extant books during the Guangxu period. In July of this year, Mr. Cai Yuanpei of the Academia Sinica and Mr. Ye Yuhu, the former Minister of Railways, and others initiated the revision of the catalogue. Zhao Wanli, a compiler from the Beiping Library, has been jointly organized by the committee to sort it out. There are many cases of books without catalogues in the pavilion, and there are also many cases of books without catalogues. Fortunately, the lost books are said to still be in the collections of public and private individuals in our country, and have not yet flowed overseas to foreign lands. If it is possible to donate money to spare, in addition to the repair work, collecting the lost old books would be a great pleasure for the literary world. This is the extravagant hope of the committee members, and it is also what the sages of our country deeply sympathize with. We are looking forward to hearing from you. Sincerely, Feng Zhenqun, Chairman of the Yin County Literature Committee, and members Xin Jiangming, Wu Jingxiong, Xia Qiyu, Sun Zhenqi, Ma Heng, Ma Ying, Ma Lian, Chen Xunzheng, Chen Baolin, Chen Xunci, Zhang Shouyong, Zhang Qin, Zhang Chuanbao, Zhang Zhiming, Zhang Yuanwei, Zhang Jin, Zhang Qijun, Ye Qianliang, Zhao Jiasun, Li Yan, Wei Jiong, and 103 others. Anglo-American War Debt Negotiations

Stabilizing Currency Values Discussed First 72

Reuters, Washington, 10th - Anglo-American war debt negotiations began today, and it seems that the first issue discussed was the stabilization of currency values. The Shang Bao newspaper said that the U.S. dollar and the British pound could be stabilized at two-thirds of their former gold parity. The New York Times said that it is now certain that the idea of ​​amortizing war debts with a round sum of one-tenth cannot be accepted. If the negotiations have not ended by the next payment date, which is around December 15, then Britain can still make a payment in accordance with the silver payment method in June to show its creditworthiness. The Times also said that President Roosevelt has an elusive attitude towards the war debt issue, and the attitude of American officials resembles sympathetic onlookers, so the burden of negotiation now falls on the British representative.

Fang Zhenwu's Representative Guo Yunlong Arrives in Beiping, Makes Extravagant Demands, Tang and Liu's Troops Continue to Advance South, Frontline Sentries Still in Contact 73

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang, together with the troops of Tang Yulin, Liu Guitang, and Wang Ying, are advancing south again. The eastern route has advanced to Da Xiaodongliu, approaching Gaoliying, while the western route has occupied Da Xiaotang. He Yingqin, the acting chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, has recently telegraphed Fang three times, advising him to cease military operations. Fang then sent Councilor Guo Yunlong on the 8th, carrying a personal letter, to Beiping to visit He. The following are the texts of the communications between He and Fang: (1) He's telegram to Fang: "Commander Fang, Uncle Ping, I have received your telegram. I believe you have received my telegram. I ordered the troops on the front line to stop attacking yesterday morning. I hope you will send a responsible representative to Beiping to discuss matters as soon as possible. Everything is fine. He Yingqin, Yu Shen (2) Fang's letter: "Minister He, respected sir, I am stationed in Matun, and things are out of my control. I have no other intentions. I am grateful for your kindness in mediating and finding a solution that benefits both sides. I dare not disobey your orders. However, Zhongfu (Wang) is detained due to an incident, and Yun Sheng (Meng) has gone elsewhere for a reason. I am sending Guo Yunlong to pay my respects on my behalf, convey my sincerity, and discuss everything. I respectfully ask for your sincerity and guidance. Both public and private affairs are deeply appreciated. I express my sincere respect. Fang Zhenwu, 8th"

Guo arrived at the defense area of ​​a certain regiment of Wan Fulin's troops stationed in Mafang at 4:00 PM on the 8th, carrying a white flag and accompanied by more than 20 cavalrymen. The garrison initially suspected trickery, but Guo dismissed the cavalry and came south alone with one attendant, explaining his intentions. The garrison agreed to allow him to pass through, and the regimental commander sent him to the division headquarters in Pingfang. Guo met with Division Commander Zhu Hongxun and that night Zhu sent two cars to send him to the Western Suburb military headquarters. Yesterday morning (the 9th) he entered the city and visited He at the Jurentang at 9:00 AM. He was meeting with Sugimura and could not receive him personally, so he sent Wang Lun to meet him instead. This afternoon (the 10th), He summoned Guo for a face-to-face meeting. It is reported that Guo will return to Tangshan in one or two days to report back. Fang has made extravagant demands, including several items: (1) Hoping that the authorities will improve politics (2) His troops will be reorganized into an army (3) He himself will be a soldier and is willing to work hard for the country and lead his troops to defend the country. He's only condition for Fang is to leave the army. Since Fang refuses to resign, the gap between the two sides' opinions is too wide to negotiate. However, He is eager to cease military operations as soon as possible, and the other side has also proposed several items for earnest consultation: (1) If Fang can leave the army, then everything can be discussed (2) Personal safety is absolutely guaranteed (3) The troops are designated to gather at a specific location, and personnel will be assigned to edit them. It is also planned to send a representative to accompany Fang's representative Guo Yunlong to meet with Fang to discuss matters. What the outcome will be in the future is difficult to predict, but based on observations from all sides, it is feared that a solution will not be easily reached.

Since the day before yesterday, the war on the front line has entered a state of ceasefire, but the Fang-Ji side is digging trenches and mobilizing troops, which is extremely busy. It was also reported last night that the troops of Tang Yulin and Liu Guitang, etc., are now entering the Great Wall from the Erdaoguan Taolin Pass area one after another. After the majority of the Tang and Liu forces arrive, Fang and Ji will take action. Whether or not this is reliable remains to be proven by facts. At 9:00 PM last night, Fang and Ji also sent a small number of cavalry to attack the Gaoliying and Daxiaodongliu areas, firing hundreds of shots. The garrison suddenly heard the gunshots and also fired artillery in response. The Fang troops then retreated. At the same time, Fang troops' cavalry were also found in the Nanguanzhuang and Dongxiguanzhuang areas of Gaoliying, appearing and disappearing unpredictably in various villages. This morning, the sentries on both sides had minor contact in the Mafang area. The garrison is currently building fortifications for defense. (October 10)

Northern Route Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression Gu Zhutong Will Take Office — General Headquarters' Organization is Continuing, Will Move to the Front — 74

Nanchang Communication: The military affairs of suppressing the Red Army in five provinces are well under way in all aspects of deployment. The northern route is the main force in the five-province campaign against the Red Army as it faces the Red bandits directly, and its importance is even greater. However, Northern Route Commander-in-Chief Liu Zhi has not yet taken office in Jiangxi due to the importance of military and political affairs in Henan. Everything went smoothly with Gu. Gu sent people to the province to organize the headquarters. Chiang Orders the Hubei Provincial Government to Reform the Decadent Customs of Southern Hubei. The Provincial Government Entrusts the Civil Affairs, Education, and Construction Departments to Formulate Measures. 75

Hankou Communication: The political corruption and lazy customs of Hubei Province are most prominent in the seven counties of western Hubei, such as Shihe, where the wealthy bully the people, finances are chaotic, education is bankrupt, and opium is rampant. After the provincial government conducted an inspection, all the states were announced, and plans were being formulated to organize them. It was unexpected that the various properties in southern Hubei were no less than those in western Hubei. The Western Route Headquarters of the Five-Province Bandit Suppression Army, which uses southern Hubei as its suppression area, recently sent Liu Wonan, Yi Baigeng, and others to Tongcheng, Tongshan, Chongyang, Puchi, and Xianning to conduct field inspections. The results obtained are as follows: (1) Finance: Municipal tickets are rampant, finances are chaotic, and the allocation of land per mu in each district is unavoidable to cause disturbance. (2) Construction: Highways and county roads have mostly not started construction, and guard work is also lax. No attention has been paid to wasteland reclamation and afforestation. (3) Education: Social education institutions are all lacking. There are no new-style schools, and there are not many private schools. Most of the people are illiterate. (4) Public Security: There is no plan for suppressing thieves and bandits, and there are no sanitation facilities. People are mostly addicted to opium and gambling. The public security authorities either collect lamp donations and land donations, or collect a license fee of five yuan per person. There is also a license public fee, and each license must pay one thousand yuan before being allowed to operate. Those who commit private smoking and gambling are arrested and fined before being released. At the same time, Commander-in-Chief Jiang also reported that the people of southern Hubei are lazy and corrupt, and particularly addicted to smoking and gambling. He recently sent a telegram from Nanchang ordering the Hubei Provincial Government to find ways to revitalize and reorganize the government in order to change the decadent customs. After receiving the order, the provincial government submitted it to the political affairs meeting on the 6th for discussion and decided to entrust it to the three departments of civil affairs, education, and construction to formulate concrete measures based on the principles instructed by Commander-in-Chief Jiang in the telegram, and submit them for verification and implementation. (9th)

The Military Affairs of Bandit Suppression in the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are Proceeding Smoothly. Nearly 4,000 Guns Have Been Issued on All Routes. The Bandits Have Suffered Heavy Losses. Post-Disaster Relief is Being Organized in the Border Area. The Use of Funds Has Been Determined. Zhang Qun Has Suspended His Inspection Tour. The Directors of the Various Departments Will Set Off Immediately. 76

Hankou Communication: The military affairs of bandit suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have been progressing considerably in the past two months under the supervision of Liu Zhenhua, Xu Yuanquan, and Chen Jicheng. In addition to capturing and killing Red bandits, many weapons have also been seized. According to the headquarters' investigation and statistics, the troops on all routes have seized approximately 4,000 guns, all of which have been ordered by the headquarters to be submitted and appropriate bonuses will be awarded separately. Red bandits regard weapons and ammunition as treasures because they are difficult to replenish. During combat, they would rather sacrifice many lives than abandon a gun. The large-scale seizure of weapons shows the depth of the damage they have suffered. The bandits in the border area have suffered the greatest losses among all factions and have now collapsed. Liu Zhenhua is actively organizing post-disaster relief and will abolish the border area headquarters after the remaining bandits have been cleared. A post-disaster relief office will be established instead. During the transition period, a post-disaster relief preparatory office will be established to preside over the office. The total amount of funds had been previously set at 490,000 yuan and its use has now been determined and distributed in advance, divided into two major categories: expenditures and circulation. Expenditures are divided into two categories: relief and construction. Relief includes (1) reception costs of 200,000 yuan, (2) emergency relief costs of 300,000 yuan, (3) work relief costs of 400,000 yuan (4) rehabilitation costs of 40,000 yuan (5) resettlement costs of 60,000 yuan. Construction includes (1) rural construction costs of 850,000 yuan (2) self-cultivating farmer creation costs of 750,000 yuan, totaling 2,600,000 yuan. Circulation is divided into two categories: land consolidation and rural recovery (1) self-cultivating farmer loans of 1,000,000 yuan (2) industrial and commercial cooperative loans of 300,000 yuan (3) reclamation advances of 1,000,000 yuan, totaling 2,300,000 yuan. Among them, the expenditure part needs to raise a base amount in order to prepare for expenditure, while the circulation part is prepared in full by financial institutions. After the advances are disbursed, they will be recovered within a certain period, without the need to raise another base amount.

Hubei Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Qun originally planned to tour various places, recover the bandit areas, and personally inquire about the hardships of the people. However, he is now serving concurrently as the Chief of Staff of the General Headquarters, and is busy with military affairs and has no time to tour. He has cancelled the previous proposal. Meng Guangpeng, Director of Civil Affairs, and Cheng Qibao, Director of Education, will set off to eastern Hubei in the next few days to inspect and visit Liu Zhenhua in Huangchuan to discuss the implementation of special politics and education. At the same time, Li Fanyi, Director of the Construction Department, will set off to southern Hubei to inspect the construction of roads. Fan Xixu, Director of the Security Office, will also go to western Hubei again to assist Xu Yuanquan in handling the post-disaster relief in Shihe counties. (October 9)

A Large Batch of Ancient Shang Dynasty Artifacts Discovered in Shou County, Currently 787 Pieces Stored in the County Government, Provincial Government Orders the County to Transport Them All to the Provincial Capital for Storage 77

Anqing Communication: The discovery of unearthed antiquities in Zhujiaji, Shou County, northern Anhui, has been widely rumored for a long time. A month ago, Chen Dongyuan, the director of the provincial library, submitted a request to the Department of Education to forward it to the provincial government, ordering Xi Chulin, the administrative inspector and concurrently the county magistrate of the fourth district, and also Zhu Hongchu, a local gentry, to quickly hand over all the antiquities excavated and transport them to the province for preservation. The matter was delayed for a month without a response. Subsequently, the provincial government ordered Liu Fupeng, a librarian from the library, to go to the county for investigation. He then went to investigate with County Commissioner Wu Ziming and others. It is said that the place where the villagers excavated this time is called Li San Gu Dui. Since the end of the second month of the old lunar calendar to the fifth leap month of this year, more than 150 villagers jointly elected eleven people as team leaders and cooperated in excavation for more than three months. They dug a pit more than six or seven zhang deep and more than two zhang in diameter, with a total of three layers inside, separated by large pieces of wood. Each layer contained antiquities. The format should be a large underground warehouse rather than an ancient tomb. The excavated antiquities have been sold for fifty-one pieces, including sixteen bronze tripods, eight jade oxen, and five bronze jue, etc., with very high prices. The villagers only sold them for 2,995 yuan and divided them among themselves as labor and food costs. There are still a very large number of remaining antiquities scattered among local gentry and primary schools. After Liu and others inspected, registered, and sealed them, the county government took them all back. It is estimated that there are currently 787 pieces temporarily stored in the county government, including more than 20 ancient tripods, as well as large pieces of jade jue, jade bricks, and jade stones. In addition, there are daily utensils such as teacups, rice bowls, pots, basins, rulers, and stools, as well as tool utensils such as shovels, saws, knives, axes, hooks, and bores, and military utensils such as swords, spears, arrowheads, and gun molds. In general, the value of the unearthed antiquities this time and the large number of them are unprecedented in decades. It is said that one of the tripods originally had tadpole characters engraved on it, and there was a knife-engraved record of the collection time underneath, and the text was also very old. There is no doubt that it was a relic of the Shang Dynasty that was hidden during the Eastern Zhou Dynasty. Liu has returned to the province a few days ago and submitted a list to the provincial government. The library believes that the matter concerns ancient culture and should be organized and researched as soon as possible for the public. It has submitted a request to the provincial government for verification and instructions. The educational circles Cheng Yansheng, Yao Zhongshi, Yu Youquan, Xu Yandong, Cao Chixia, and Cheng Xiaosu also jointly submitted a request to the provincial government, requesting that the county be ordered to send all the antiquities to the province and hand them over to the library for safekeeping, so that they can be viewed by the majority of people. The provincial government yesterday replied and ordered the county to comply with the order, find ways to recover the sold antiquities, carefully transport the existing antiquities to the province, and strictly prohibit any private excavation and sale in the future. (October 9)

Shandong Provincial Government Takes Over Changshan Islands, Administrative Commissioner Zhang Xiangwu Reports to Jinan 78

Jinan Communication: In the coastal area of eastern Shandong, there are numerous islands with abundant marine resources. Just in Penglai County alone, there are more than ten islands, commonly known as the "Eight Islands of Penglai," referring to the eight larger ones. Because the largest of these is Changshan Island, it is also known as the Changshan Islands. This area is located in deep sea, and transportation is inconvenient, so there are occasional threats from bandits. Five or six years ago, it was under the administration of the Bohai Navy. Now that the navy has been downsized, the administrative rights have been handed back to the Shandong Provincial Government. Chairman Han Fuqu has appointed Zhang Xiangwu, the General Commander of the Fifth Route National Army, to concurrently serve as Administrative Commissioner. After receiving the appointment, Zhang has already gone to take over and inspect the area. Yesterday (the 7th), Zhang came to Jinan from Penglai to meet with Han and report on the progress. According to Zhang, "These islands are located deep in the sea, guarding the gateway to the Bohai Sea. Changshan Island is the largest and closest to the mainland, with a north-south diameter of eighteen li and an east-west width of seven or eight li, thirty li from Penglai, and more than two thousand households. During my inspection, I visited Changshan Island, Miao Island, Daheishan Island, Xiaoheishan Island, Ji Island, Gaoshan Island, Daqin Island, Xiaoqin Island, Nancheng Huang Island, and Beicheng Huang Island. Apart from Changshan Island, which has the largest area and population, the others vary in size, with populations ranging from three to five hundred households, or dozens of households. One island has only one household, with four or five people, young and old, who live by fishing. The northernmost is Beicheng Huang Island, which is two hundred and several tens of li from Penglai County, one hundred and sixty li north of Lushun, and six hundred and eighty li from Dalian, making it closer to Shandong. These islands were originally managed by the Navy, which dispatched a counselor to manage affairs and established a public security bureau with more than forty policemen on Changshan Island. After taking over, it is planned to abolish the public security bureau to reduce the burden on the residents. If necessary, the local militia will be stationed. In the future, the expenses for the development of these islands will be planned by the provincial government, without placing the burden on the local areas. Various types of fish, sea cucumbers, and shrimp are abundant on the islands, and the products are of excellent quality." (8th)

The Revenue Police Headquarters of the Ministry of Finance stationed in Suzhou has been ordered to go to Jiangxi to carry out bandit suppression work. Wuxi

Wuxi Barbers Reduce Prices and Strike 80

In recent years, the social economy has been in a state of panic, and all industries have been in decline. The barber industry has also suffered a great decline. Recently, in order to attract customers, they have posted large red price reduction papers on the glass windows, marking the prices. Western style is 300 wen, monk's head is 200 wen, shaving is 120 wen. Business is gradually turning around, but this has caused disputes among the industry. After mediation by the county party headquarters, they still operate according to the old rules. Recently, barber shops in the Zhoushanbang Tonghui Road area have reduced prices again due to the failure of business to improve. However, the income of barber shop partners has been greatly affected, and they have unanimously expressed their opposition. The shop owners have ignored this, so all partners have issued secret signals on the night before yesterday at about 9 o'clock to carry out a strike. After receiving the report, Zhang Shiquan and Jin Yuan, members of the Barber Industry Association, were deeply afraid that the situation would expand. They held a temporary emergency meeting at the Bajie Lane Clubhouse at 2 pm yesterday (11th). More than 40 people, including Zhang Zhenhong, attended. The county party also sent Gao Zugao, an officer, to attend the mediation. After deliberation, it was decided to send representatives Zhou Shaoqin and others to the second branch of the Public Security Bureau to ask the owner of the Hengda Barber Shop, Sha Laoer, who first posted the price reduction paper, to be brought to justice. The acting director of the Cheng branch sent patrol officer Xiao Tongsheng to remove the posted papers, and advised all shops to remove all price reduction papers. However, the shops that reduced prices have very firm will. It is not known how the price reduction strike will be resolved.

Nantong Exempts Additional Taxes Along the River for Ten Years 81

The land along the Liuhai Sandbar is currently suffering from severe collapse, and the cost of embankment maintenance is high. It has also been hit by tidal disasters, and farmers are unable to bear the burden. The financial department has already found out that the county additional taxes will be temporarily exempted for a period of ten years. After the embankment maintenance is completed, it will be collected again.

The headquarters of the Fourth District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police moved to Nantong during the Shanghai war. Gaoyou Security Corps Captures Bandits and Liberates the County 83

Baizhao Village in the seventh district of the county was suddenly attacked by four bandit ships the day before yesterday, carrying more than 20 bandits. More than ten bandits, armed with box guns, landed on shore and began searching each household. The village's security chief, Wu Yin, sounded the gong to raise the alarm, and led seven men to pursue and intercept the bandits. They intercepted two bandit ships near Dianduo and captured eight bandits, including Yang Zigao, Wang Xiang, Wu Caohua, and Wu Guoyuan. They were sent to the county yesterday for interrogation.

Grain Ship Capsizes in Hurricane 84

Wang Yunhai, a grain merchant from Leping Township in the twelfth district of the county, loaded a boat of wheat in Jingou Town, intending to sell it in the city. However, when traveling in the lake, it suddenly encountered a hurricane and capsized. All ships tried their best to rescue the four people from the water. They were fortunate to be reborn, but all the wheat has been swept away by the waves. It is said that the losses are huge.

Pinghu's New Jiaju Ferry Continues to Cause Trouble 85

The Zhapu ferry "New Jiaju" caused Xu Renhe, a farmer from Xiaogang in Donghu, to fall into the water and have his head cut off by the propeller, resulting in immediate death. The police detained the ship's captain and sent him to the county. Unexpectedly, a day later, the ship was preparing to depart from the Ximen Wharf in Zhapu to the city. Passengers had not yet boarded safely when the ship suddenly sailed, causing an old woman to fall into the river. Fortunately, there were many people at the wharf who had not yet dispersed, and they immediately jumped into the water to rescue her, and she was fortunate to be reborn, but she was completely soaked and barely breathing.

Water Police Team Kills a Large Number of Pirates; Huang Xinong, patrol officer of the second squad of the second brigade of the Zhenhai Water Police, 87

led three patrol boats on a patrol on the sea the day before yesterday (4th). They encountered three pirate ships in the waters of Dog's Head Mountain. The pirate leader, nicknamed "Red-Haired Three Heads," had more than 50 pirates. The police immediately opened fire, and the pirates returned fire. After two hours of fierce fighting, the pirates suffered heavy casualties and were unable to sustain the fight. They raised their sails and tried to escape, but the police bravely pursued and surrounded the pirate ships. Seeing that the situation was not good, more than ten pirates jumped into the sea to commit suicide. Four more vicious pirates in the boats surrendered. Five policemen were seriously injured by bullets, and two refugees were killed or injured. More than 20 refugees were rescued. The four pirates captured were sent to the Zhenhai Brigade headquarters yesterday for investigation.

Xiaoshan County Magistrate Goes to Villages to Investigate Locust Plague 88

Locusts were discovered in Shimen in the southern part of Xiaoshan County a month ago, obscuring the sky and devouring much of the rice crops. Villagers tried their best to control the plague, but with little effect, resulting in a disaster and reduced autumn harvest. County Magistrate Zhang, concerned about the people's food, went to the Shimen area on the morning of the 7th to investigate the disaster in order to find ways to provide relief.

Mingguang Stops Pre-Borrowing of Second Term Land Tax 89

The county government previously issued bonds for the second term land tax due to financial difficulties and borrowed them from various districts. Continuous Rain Damages Crops 90

Recent continuous rain has lasted for more than ten days. At this time of harvest, the damage to crops is very serious. Mung beans are moldy and early rice is germinating. It is said that the harvest will be reduced by 30% to 40%.

Letter from the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways 91

Dear Editor,

Regarding the editorial "Japanese Coal and National Coal" in your newspaper on October 4 this year, the article stated that Chinese coal production has "excessively high transportation costs." It also mentioned that at the beginning of the Republic of China, state-owned railways had special pricing arrangements for coal transportation, which enabled the development of various mines in the north. However, the special prices for coal transportation were successively canceled, and all coal was uniformly classified into the sixth class. Although there have been several reductions since then, the transportation costs are still 70% to 80% higher than before. Increased transportation costs are the "reason" for the gradual reduction in Chinese coal production. This is not in accordance with the facts. Although the establishment of modern coal mines in our country dates back to the early years of Guangxu, they were poorly managed or entrusted to the wrong people, resulting in the depletion of capital and difficulty in continuing. By the last years of the Qing Dynasty, foreign capital was attracted, resulting in joint ventures. In addition to the Kailuan Mining Company at the beginning of the Republic of China, the Liugou, Lincheng, Jingxing, and Yingdong mines were all in the hands of foreigners. The Zhongxing and other mines were still in their infancy with limited production. The only mines run by Chinese were the Pingxiang, Baojin, and many small kilns. Since the reform, the Chinese have gradually recognized the necessity of independently operating mines. Foreign-funded coal mines have been recovered from time to time, and commercial coal mines have been gradually established. Small mines that originally used local methods of mining have also adopted machinery or merged into modern mines. Mines with domestic capital have only recently shown signs of revitalization. They have not been hindered in their development due to excessively high transportation costs. For example, the Liugou Mine only cleared the arrears in the eighth year of the Republic of China, and its production and sales reached more than 740,000 tons in the seventh year, setting a new record for the mine. Another example is the Zhongxing Coal Mine, which added 800,000 taels of capital in the 31st year of Guangxu, and by the 16th year of the Republic of China, its assets had reached 15 million yuan. Recently, it has planned to produce 4,000 to 6,000 tons of coal per day, becoming a large mine. Other mines in Datong, Jin, Yu, Su, Wan, Xiang, and Yue have recently been organized or are just beginning to sprout. The large mines run by Chinese are developing and have not reduced their mining due to increased transportation costs. What is regrettable is that the civil war has been frequent, coal transportation has been difficult, Pingxiang has been plagued by communist bandits and has been on the verge of bankruptcy for a long time, and coal mines in the east were once on par with foreign coal, but since the September 18th Incident, they have suddenly become objects of foreign dumping. These are all political problems and not transportation cost problems. As for transportation costs, the Ministry has always maintained a policy of protecting national coal. Railway freight is only divided into six classes, and coal is included in the lowest class, originally at the same lowest cost as mud, sand, and stone. However, in practice, the coal transportation costs of various railways vary depending on transportation conditions and cost factors. However, most coal-producing railways have special prices or discounts, often charging extremely low prices, even below the transportation costs of mud, sand, and stone, and far below transportation costs. It has never been uniformly classified into the sixth class. Recently, in order to maintain the dumping of foreign coal, the Ministry has specifically maintained it. In addition to repeatedly suspending the addition of coal transportation prices on various railways, the Pinghan, Xiang, E, Jiaoji, and Pingsui Railways have either been given special reductions or discounts. For example, the current price for transporting coal from Liugou to Hankou on the Pinghan Railway is only 5 yuan and 9 jiao per ton, and the recent special price is only 5 yuan and 3 jiao, which is still lower than the lowest special price of 5 yuan and 3 jiao and 4 fen enjoyed by the mine. If calculated according to the sixth class of goods on the railway, the charge should be 17 yuan and 7 fen. The current transportation cost is only 35% of the sixth class, and the special price is less than one-third of the sixth class. As for the old special price, it was only used for powerful large mines that started at the time when foreigners were running mines in North China, and the mines run by Chinese were not included. Now, all mines, large and small, are treated equally, and have the opportunity for balanced development. Recently, gold prices have soared, and labor and materials have increased several times. Operating expenses are far beyond what they were twenty years ago. However, the transportation costs of coal on various railways have not only not increased but have decreased. What is regrettable is that many national coal mines are located inland, and transportation is difficult. Also, due to poor management or lack of capital, production is not abundant and expenses are too heavy. The cost per ton is often several times higher than that of foreign coal or coal mined by foreign capital. Even compared to the same mine several years ago, the cost is more than double. The fundamental solution to the national coal problem lies in expanding production, reducing costs, increasing tariffs, implementing dumping taxes, and reducing various improper expenses. The coal industry operated by our country is still in its infancy and needs to be emulated and implemented to maintain it. Your newspaper is concerned about the coal industry, which is deeply appreciated. However, you may not be fully aware of the details of transportation costs. I hope you will publish this letter to prevent misunderstandings. Sincerely, Business Department of the Ministry of Railways, October 9.

Local News

Grand National Day Celebration Held the Day Before Yesterday; The City Party Department Convened a Commemorative Meeting with Representatives from All Walks of Life, Reaching Over Two Hundred People 92

For this year's Double Ten Festival, the central government, due to the national crisis, issued an order to the whole country not to be extravagant. Therefore, the City Party Department of this city convened a National Day Commemorative Meeting for representatives from all walks of life at 9:30 am on the morning of the celebration. Over two hundred people attended. The chairman, Cai Hongtian, reported on the significance of the celebration. Details of the various activities are recorded as follows:

Order of the Meeting: (1) Opening; (2) Singing the Party Song; (3) Giving the highest salute to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister; (4) Reading the Prime Minister's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) Report; (7) Speech; (8) Shouting slogans; (9) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report: After performing the rituals, the chairman reported that today is the National Day of the Republic of China, the 22nd anniversary. Twenty-two years ago, on this day, the martyrs of our Party launched an uprising in Wuchang, overthrowing the Qing Dynasty and establishing the Republic of China. Recalling the last three years of the Qing Dynasty, due to the corruption of the political system, it was repeatedly subjected to aggression by various imperialists, leading to the decline of people's livelihoods and the weakening of the nation. The late Prime Minister, seeing this, realized that without implementing a revolution, the country would not survive or be saved. After several struggles, with an indomitable spirit, he persevered and launched an uprising in Wuchang twenty-two years ago, and the Republic of China was established. The tenth of October was designated as National Day. This day is the most glorious day in the history of the Party and the nation, and it is worthy of our enthusiastic celebration. However, this year's National Day is faced with both external regrets and internal chaos. We were ordered not to be extravagant, so we are celebrating very simply. But the significance of celebrating National Day is not in the form. Furthermore, the Chinese nation has experienced several crises. In the past twenty-two years, we do not know how much of our good land has been lost. Now, the banditry has not yet been suppressed, and the Japanese are still inching forward step by step, repeatedly invading. Under these circumstances, the Chinese people should quickly wake up. Therefore, today, celebrating National Day means celebrating on one hand and working hard for the country on the other, jointly seeking ways to strengthen the nation and paying attention to (1) the revival of the countryside, (2) the construction of national transportation, (3) the promotion of national goods, and (4) the consolidation of national defense, etc. Then he shouted slogans and adjourned the meeting.

Meeting Slogans: (1) Actively produce and enrich national power; (2) Suppress the Red bandits and stabilize society; (3) Prepare to recover lost territories with strength; (4) Support the government in implementing construction work; (5) Down with Japanese imperialism; (6) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (7) Long live the Republic of China.

Slogan Highlights: (1) October 10th is the glorious anniversary of the revival of the Chinese nation; (2) Commemorating National Day means working hard to resist Japan, avenge shame, and seek revenge; (3) Support the government and implement construction work; (4) Commemorating National Day is a commemoration of the Party's Xinhai Revolution overthrowing the Qing Dynasty; (5) Unite sincerely to ensure peace and unity; (6) Commemorating National Day means actively producing and enriching national power; (7) Commemorating National Day means not forgetting the hardships created by the Prime Minister and all the martyrs; (8) Commemorating National Day means preparing to recover lost territories; (9) Commemorating National Day means suppressing the Red bandits and stabilizing society; (10) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (11) Long live the Republic of China.

All Chinese and Western guests took off their hats and filed in. Mayor Wu then ascended to the auditorium and unveiled the bronze commemorative plaque embedded inside, which read: "Completion Ceremony of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, October 10, 1933, Republic of China." By the time the monument was unveiled, it was already 10:30 am. Mayor Wu went upstairs to broadcast a report.

Mayor's Report on Construction Plans 98

Distinguished guests, today the Shanghai Municipal Government is holding a ceremony for the completion of its new building, and we are greatly honored by the presence and guidance of Chinese and foreign guests. I have been in charge of this city for less than two years. At the beginning of my tenure, I encountered the Shanghai Incident. I have tried my best to be loyal and to cope with the difficulties. I am grateful for the joint cooperation and assistance of local worthies and foreign friends, which has fortunately restored peace to Shanghai and stabilized the order of the city. As we hold such a grand ceremony here today, recalling the painful past years, I still feel infinitely saddened. Entrusted with heavy responsibilities by the Party and the State, and with the earnest expectations of the citizens, I have never dared to forget the suffering of my citizens in this difficult and arduous process, and I have never ceased to actively plan the restoration of the war zone. Day and night, I have strived to do my best for the welfare of my citizens and the relief of my disaster-stricken people. All kinds of plans have been drafted or implemented. Although there have been no special achievements due to financial and time constraints, I will always strive to live up to the expectations of my citizens. As for the difficult construction process of the new municipal building and its profound and great significance, I have given a detailed and thorough account in my article "The Starting Point and Significance of the Construction of the Central District of Shanghai," which was published in today's newspapers. Here, I can only briefly explain my feelings in a few points. First, the construction of Greater Shanghai is based on the construction plan of our Party's General Secretary. The construction of the central district is the first step towards completing the plan for Greater Shanghai. The completion of the new municipal government building today is the starting point for the construction of the central district. Each of the previous mayors of Greater Shanghai, Mr. Huang Yingbai, Mr. Zhang Boxuan, and Mr. Zhang Yuejun, painstakingly planned and painstakingly managed the project. The results of their efforts have created the rudimentary form of today. Today, on the one hand, I represent the citizens in expressing my respect to the previous mayors, and on the other hand, I will carry on the spirit of the previous mayors and strive to engage in the construction of Greater Shanghai in order to realize the legacy of General Secretary. (Top) Mayor Wu and his wife (photographed by Xu Tianzhang) (Bottom) Military police regiment parade (photographed by Qichang Photo Studio)

Second, given the complexity and scale of the Greater Shanghai plan, the new municipal government building can only be considered a drop in the ocean. However, the current location of the city center, close to Wusong in the north, bordering the concession in the south, facing the Huangpu River in the east, and adjacent to the railway in the west, is strategically located and conveniently accessible. In the years to come, there will be considerable development and prosperity. I sincerely hope that the citizens of Shanghai will have confidence in themselves and not rely on the already established constructions of others. We should rise up and create a new world of prosperity and development, so as to demonstrate the inherent creative cultural capacity of our Chinese nation. Observing the past efforts of the citizens of Shanghai in the construction of Shanghai, I also firmly believe that in the future, we will be able to make this city the most sound and prosperous metropolis. Third, Shanghai is the center of national economy and culture, and also one of the world's major cities. China is now in the process of construction. On the negative side, we should eliminate all obstacles to construction. On the positive side, we should actively plan the advancement of the new China's construction plan. The most important aspect of the construction of the new China,

is nothing more than the development of politics and economy. The characteristics of a city are that on the one hand, it is the birthplace of a country's democratic politics, and on the other hand, it is the driving force behind a country's economic development. I am willing to work together with the citizens of Jinshi to promote the rapid development of Greater Shanghai and its increasing prosperity. Mayor Inspects Troops, Impressive Military Appearance 99

At 10:30 AM, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, accompanied by inspecting officers Yang Hu, Wen Hongen, Wang Yiting, Wang Binyan, etc., ascended the command platform and began the troop inspection. First, Commander Qi Xueqi reported the number of troops to Inspecting Officer, then Inspecting Officer Mayor Wu, accompanying Inspecting Officer Yang Huchang (Hu), Director Wen (Hongen), Deputy Adjutant Wen (Jiangang), and Wang Binyan, head of the Security Regiment, conducted an inspection. Then, they returned to the command platform. The Mayor stood in the center, with the accompanying Inspecting Officers lined up on the left and right. After the Commander issued the order, military music was played, and the military police marched forward in formation, passing in front of the command platform for a review. The inspected troops included: First group, two platoons of training soldiers from the Security Department; Second group, the first infantry regiment of the Security Department, one platoon of Mauser pistol soldiers; Third group, one platoon of pursuit artillery from the Security Department; Fourth group, one platoon of armored bicycle soldiers from the Security Department; Fifth group, two platoons of infantry from the Public Security Bureau's police brigade, one platoon of machine gunners; Sixth group, two battalions of the Security Regiment. The city's boy scouts and firefighters also joined the inspection. Finally, the parade was concluded with a procession promoting domestic products. During the inspection, Chinese and foreign guests were present to watch, with Western guests on the right and Chinese guests on the left. All the military police were neatly dressed, in high spirits, and marched in a very orderly manner, making for an impressive military appearance.

Ceremony Concludes with Cheers of "Long Live" 100

After the troop inspection was completed, music was played and the ceremony concluded. Then, Mayor Wu led everyone in chanting "Long Live Shanghai," "Long Live the Chinese Kuomintang," and "Long Live the Republic of China." After the cheers, Chinese and foreign guests returned to their respective homes.

Firefighting Demonstration Showcases Excellent Skills 101

In addition to participating in the parade, the city's fire brigades also demonstrated their skills in the square in front of the city government at 2 PM in the afternoon. In advance, two four-story high buildings were erected with reed mats on the open space. During the demonstration, thirty gallons of gasoline were poured on them, and the buildings were filled with flammable materials. Some firefighters, disguised as residents, were pre-positioned inside the buildings and set off sulfur gunpowder. In an instant, thick smoke billowed from each window, and flames soared into the sky, as if thousands of fire dragons were rising into the air. The fire was fierce, and the firefighters worked hard to install hoses and carry out rescue operations. Other firefighters used ladders to jump into the windows and rescue the disguised residents pre-positioned in the buildings. Some firefighters climbed onto the roof and used water to extinguish the fire. One firefighter jumped down from a high place to rescue people. After about half an hour, the fire was completely extinguished, and the audience applauded continuously, which showed the progress of the city's firefighting efforts.

Mayor's Speech: Service and Sacrifice 102

After the firefighting demonstration, Mayor Wu convened all the firefighters and gave a speech.

He said that the Shanghai Fire Brigade is one of the citizens' autonomous organizations and has a long history. Since the establishment of the municipal government, it has assisted us and made remarkable achievements. The spirit of the Fire Brigade is one of service and one of sacrifice. I hope that the citizens of Shanghai will always adhere to the spirit of service and sacrifice in their efforts to establish fire brigades, complete autonomy, assist in the construction of a new Shanghai, and then build a new China. Shanghai is the economic and cultural center of the country, and it has a great responsibility to the country. I hope that the citizens of Shanghai will take the task of saving the country as their own responsibility.

It was to seek the revival of the nation, which aroused the jealousy of the Qing government. Song's Trip to Nanjing Temporarily Postponed 110

New loan negotiations with the banking community using surplus New Treasury Bonds as collateral. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen was originally scheduled to take a flight to Nanjing on the morning of the 9th to attend a meeting of the Executive Yuan. Chiang Kai-shek's Sikorsky aircraft was also ordered to come to Shanghai on the 8th to await Minister Song's arrival. It is now known that Mr. Song has been conducting various important financial matters in Shanghai for days and has not yet finished. He will not be able to leave Shanghai within the next few days, and it will probably have to be postponed until the beginning of next week before he can go to Nanjing.

According to New Sound News Agency, the Ministry of Finance issued 100 million yuan of Customs Treasury Bonds of the Republic of China in 1933. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen is in contact with the banking community in Shanghai to use the New Treasury Bonds to repay the temporary loans of various banks, and to conduct new loan negotiations. According to reliable sources in the banking community yesterday, the loan negotiations have been largely completed. The total amount is 12 million yuan, which will be undertaken separately by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the China Salt Bank, the Continental Bank, and the Jincheng Bank, and will be secured by the remaining amount of the New Treasury Bonds. However, the exact amount is still under discussion and may need to be increased to 15 million yuan.

Opening Ceremony Held 114

After the motorcade parade, the conference staff rushed to the City Chamber of Commerce. The opening ceremony was held at 2:00 PM. Luo Qinghua of the City Chamber of Commerce, Chen Yiting of the National Products Promotion Association, and representatives from various agencies, groups, and guests from all walks of life, more than 800 people, attended. After the meeting, Wu Huanru, the second section chief of the City Social Affairs Bureau, presided over the meeting and reported the purpose of the meeting. He said, "Ladies and gentlemen, we are here to hold the National Products Movement Week ceremony. If we think about it carefully, we can't help but feel heartache. The people of a country should in principle use their own country's products. But in today's China, it is necessary to hold a sports conference for people to use national products. Isn't this a heartbreaking thing? Because of China's poverty, all sectors of agriculture, industry, and commerce are seeking a way out. We must know that the alias for a way out is to solve the problem of eating. But judging from today's situation in China, where people like to use foreign goods, it is no wonder that all industries cannot be revitalized, and it is no wonder that all industries have no way out, and the problem of eating for all industries cannot be solved. On the contrary, if China can love its country and all consumption is determined to buy only national products, then at least tens of millions of yuan of foreign goods can be stopped every year. With this sum of money, how many businesses can be run and how many people in the agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors can solve the problem of eating? Therefore, at this time of national crisis, we cannot only hate the enemy's barbarity and ferocity. We must know that under today's circumstances, the Japanese are armed to the teeth because their people love their country. Therefore, if we want to eliminate this national crisis, we must love our country, and the way to love our country must start with loving and using national products." When the first National Products Movement Week was held in this city, many people said that the Chinese people's love for foreign goods is a habit, and it is not easy to change customs. But if we are fair, after several years of holding enthusiastic national products conferences, not only the citizens of this city, but also the people of the whole country, have gradually been able to arouse the concept of loving and using national products. The capitalists who invest in domestic product factories and those who run domestic product businesses are also more than in the past. It is not a good phenomenon. Only because the Chinese people's habit of loving and using national products has not yet become universal, the future of national products still has no significant acceleration. Therefore, whenever this bureau holds a National Products Movement Week, it must hold a National Products Exhibition in conjunction with it. The purpose is not only to change consumers' bad habits of using foreign goods, but also to promote producers' determination to improve and work hard to manufacture. In this movement week, in addition to motorcade parades and other programs, there is still an exhibition. The location is in the Confucius Temple Park in Xiaoximen, Nanshi. The purpose is nothing more than to cultivate the habit of loving and using national products among all circles." After the chairman's report, Luo Qinghua, the representative of the City Chamber of Commerce, gave a speech, which briefly stated, "Everyone, today is the National Day celebration, which you all know. This period is a period of national crisis, which you also understand. Today, at this time, we are holding the National Products Movement Week here, which you also understand. Therefore, today, I will briefly talk about the relationship between the National Day, the national crisis, and the National Products Movement. We recall that before September 18th of the year before last, there were still some things to celebrate every National Day. After September 18th, the January 28th Incident followed, and then the loss of Rehe and the signing of the Tanggu Truce. The national crisis deepened day by day. Since then, every time we celebrate the National Day, not only is there nothing to celebrate, but also several huge and deep wounds are added. If the Chinese people cannot work hard, the national crisis may increase every day, and there will never be a chance to commemorate the National Day. Therefore, if we want to save the national crisis, we should not want to have a good time on the National Day. Otherwise, we should all work hard and make it our goal to love the country, and the way to love the country should be to love and use national products." Then Zhang Renshi, the curator of the National Products Exhibition Hall, and Ling Yun, the representative of the Shanghai National Products Company, gave speeches. After the speeches, they continued to perform to help the fun. Three Severed Fingers and a Pool of Blood: A Body Found Floating in the Huangpu River, Missing Three Fingers; Fatal Wounds Discovered on Head and Body; Police Strive to Investigate the Truth 116

Yesterday morning at approximately 10:00 AM, detectives from the Yulin Road Police Station received a report from Qian Jinfa, a chauffeur from the Public Works Department. He stated that while passing the Qiwupu Road pier, he discovered a pool of fresh blood containing three severed fingers. He also found a trail of blood leading directly to the Huangpu River, along with three incense sticks with a paper from a lottery shop stuck in them. Upon receiving the report, the police immediately dispatched detectives to investigate and confirmed the report. However, the body was missing, presumed to have sunk to the bottom of the river. They notified the Water Police to be on the lookout for a floating corpse. At around 1:00 PM, a body was found floating near the Weituoma Road intersection. It was retrieved from the water, and the Yulin Road Police Station was notified for identification. The station then dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. The body was dressed in a black serge long gown, black woolen trousers, a white cotton short shirt, and a white cloth undershirt. It was confirmed that the hands were missing three fingers, and the severed fingers matched the wounds. A notebook found near the body contained a personal statement with the name “Shuai Shuchun,” age 29, father alive, mother deceased, one younger brother who is married but childless. It included only a few words and a telephone number. Further examination of the body revealed over a dozen fatal wounds on the head and body, indicating murder followed by disposal in the Huangpu River. The body was immediately transported to the coroner’s office, and detectives were dispatched to investigate the crime and apprehend the perpetrator.

Many Bad People in the World: A Bride Loses Her Virtue to a Villain 117

A bride runs away two days after the wedding. The groom is miserable, left with the name but not the reality. The bride was nearly abducted to Dalian. Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang, investigators from the relief association, were patrolling the docks along the Pudong riverfront at 3:00 AM yesterday morning, amidst the darkness and biting wind, to investigate any potential abduction cases on ships. On the Lian Yu steamer, which was bound for Yingkou and Dalian, at the Longmao pier, they saw a man escorting a young woman. The man spoke with a Northern accent, while the woman spoke with a Southern accent, so they asked them questions. The two claimed to be husband and wife, but their stories did not align. So, they coordinated with Bao Tan Shen Changshan from the Water Police to bring the pair to the police station. After interrogation by the police chief, the woman, aged 16, from Chongming, stated that her father's name was Shi Xiangwan. She had been betrothed since childhood to Yu Amao, the son of farmer Yu Laosan from Miaotouzhen, Zhabei District. Amao was 18 years old this year, and they were married on September 21st (August 2nd of the lunar calendar). However, her husband was base and repulsive, with an unbearable stench, so although they shared a bed after marriage, they did not consummate it. As a result, on the 24th of the same month, the third day after the wedding, she ran away. On the 5th of this month (the 16th of the lunar calendar), at 3:00 PM, she went alone to the New World company to look for her husband's younger female relatives to play with. She met this man, who gave his surname as Shi, but his given name was unknown. At 7:00 or 8:00 PM in front of the company, this man asked about her background and offered to take her to his home. They went to a hotel near Nichengqiao, but she didn't remember the room number. They stayed there for four or five days. On the first night, she was forced to take off her clothes and could not resist. She was raped seven times over the course of four or five days. Yesterday, this man asked her to go with him to Dalian to find a friend and borrow money to rent a place. He told her to say that she was his wife, 18 years old, and married last March, if anyone asked along the way or on the ship. They boarded a ship on the Huangpu River at 3:00 PM. The man's name was Shi Jinsheng, 27 years old, from Shandong, and he was unemployed. He was staying at the home of his friend Yang Jinhai on Maigen Road. He said he met the girl in front of the Wing On Company on Nanjing Road six or seven days ago, at 6:00 or 7:00 PM. He asked who she was with, and the girl said it was her brother. He invited her to go see a play, but she refused. Later, he took her to the room he had rented and raped her. They stayed there for three days, then moved to the Hongxiang Hotel, room 18, for another three days, for a total of six days. He raped her six or seven times. Yesterday, he took her on the Lianxing steamer to Dalian to find his friend Guo Chengxiang. When asked where in Dalian, he said he did not know. When asked where he got the money to go to Dalian, he said he pawned his clothes. He was ordered to be detained. Meanwhile, the investigators went to Zhabei to inform Yu Amao and Yu Laosan, who confirmed that the girl had indeed run away just two days after the wedding and that the marriage had not been consummated. They suspected that the tenant Qiu Xilin had abducted the girl after she ran away, so they had filed a complaint in the Fourth District, and the case had been transferred to the court for review. The police chief reviewed the statements and prepared a document recording the statements, which was transferred to the District Court for interrogation. After the prosecutor reviewed the case, he ordered the girl to be released to her family, and the defendant was detained pending further investigation.

Mr. Musson, a Westerner who has lived in China for many years, has collected over 300 ancient mirrors of various sizes from the Zhou and Qin dynasties onwards, as well as many types of ancient coins. Their antique charm is a magnificent sight. He previously held a public exhibition in Chicago, USA, which was well-received by the people there. Mr. Musson runs the Huoshui Garden in Shanghai, where he rehabilitates young offenders from prison. The exhibition opened on Double Ten Day and will last for four days. It has been extremely crowded with visitors every day since.

University Graduate Forges Documents and Defrauds People: A Woman from Pinghu Goes Missing, Reward Offered; University Student Impersonates Soldier to Extort Money 125

Yang Xuefang, a 13-year-old girl from Pinghu, came to Shanghai with her mother at the beginning of this month to visit relatives, the Yao Yang family, at No. 1 Guling Road. On the 5th, Yang Xuefang suddenly disappeared. After Yao Yang searched everywhere without success, she reported the incident to the Xinzha Police Station on the 6th, requesting their assistance in the search. She also distributed leaflets and posted a reward in the newspaper, offering 100 yuan to anyone who could bring Yang Xuefang back. Feng Bingsheng, a man from Changzhou, was destitute and wandering in Shanghai. After seeing the advertisement, he had a whimsical idea and saw it as a great opportunity. He forged a letter from the Hangzhou City Station Inspection Office, dressed in an old gray uniform, and impersonated a soldier from the office. On the afternoon of the 9th of this month, he went directly to the Yao Yang family, took out the letter, and claimed that the girl Yang Xuefang had been abducted by an old woman, about 50 years old, and taken by train to Hangzhou. She was discovered by the Inspection Office at the Hangzhou station and is now being held in custody. He was specially dispatched to Shanghai with the letter to notify them. If they wanted to send the girl back to Shanghai, they could. Yao Yang was overjoyed and begged Feng to send the girl back to Shanghai, offering him two yuan for travel expenses. Feng agreed and promised to bring Yang back at 4:00 PM the following day, and to collect the reward of 100 yuan. On the evening of Double Ten Day, Feng returned and took out another letter from Zhang Chuan, the captain of the Inspection Office, requesting that everything in the letter be followed. After reading the letter, Yao Yang realized that it stated that the old woman and the girl would be sent to the First Special District Court in Shanghai for interrogation, and that all travel expenses to and from Shanghai and Hangzhou must be borne by the family. After reading the letter, Yao Yang realized that Feng's actions were just empty words to deceive and extort money. She secretly reported to the police, and detective Li Wenzhao was sent to arrest Feng Bingsheng and the two letters, and took them to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, stated the case and requested that he be sentenced for fraud and forgery under Articles 363 and 214 of the Criminal Law. Yao Yang also testified about the circumstances of the fraud. Questioned, the defendant admitted that he had been persuaded by his friend Wang Xiang to take this action and claimed that he was not a vulgar person. He said that he had graduated from university and then attended military academy. He had once served in the military. His father was a judge in the military law department of the provincial government. Because he had disagreements with his family, he came to Shanghai alone and became destitute. He associated with bad friend Wang Xiang and was deceived by him. He said that he now regretted it and requested special leniency. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the statements and ordered the defendant Feng Bingsheng to be detained pending sentencing on the 16th.

An Abortive Herb 126

Although the fetus is aborted, the life is in danger. Old woman Ji Guo is detained pending investigation.

Zhu Aqiao, a 20-year-old woman from Hangzhou, who is quite beautiful, lives at No. 63 Renshou Lane, Baker Road. She works as a worker in the Shanghai Silk Weaving Factory in nearby Chunyang Lane. She recently fell in love with Xu Wenyao, the accountant of the factory.

They have an affair and she becomes pregnant. The woman is deeply afraid that her secret will be revealed and that her brother, Zhiyuan, will find out, which would be embarrassing for everyone involved. She and Xu discussed the matter and asked someone to perform an abortion. Zhu, a friend of Xu Wenyao, introduced the old woman Ji Guo from Zhabei, a Chinese area, to her. On the first of this month, in the bedroom of her friend Qian Jinmei's house at No. 51 Baker Road, it was agreed that the abortion fee would be nine yuan. An herb root, about four inches long, was inserted into Zhu's uterus. The fetus was aborted the next day, but the woman's body was exhausted. She went to the hospital for treatment. The matter was discovered by detective Zhang Degong of the Yulin Road Police Station. He arrested Ji Guo, who performed the abortion, on Xiaoshadu Road the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Xiao Xiephan interrogated her. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the case, saying that the police had sent detectives to the Shanghai Silk Weaving Factory to investigate. According to the factory, Xu Wenyao was an apprentice and had now fled without a trace. They also went to Qian Jinmei's place to inquire, and Qian said that she also worked in the factory, and that she did not know anything about Zhu Aqiao's abortion in her house, because she was working the night shift at the factory at the time. Therefore, the police did not prosecute her. The police found that Zhu was currently being treated at Guangren Hospital, and that her condition was quite serious, and that her life may be in danger. They requested a postponement. He then presented a similar herb for inspection. Zhu Zhengyuan also stated the facts of the case. When questioned, the defendant Ji Guo denied everything. Judge Xiao reviewed the statements and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody for further interrogation at a later date.

A Fierce Fight Between a Bengal Circus Tiger Mother and Son 129

During a performance on Monday night at the Haijingbo Circus, two Bengal tigers suddenly became ferocious and engaged in a fierce fight. The tiger trainers and other circus members were at a loss for what to do. They immediately fired blank shots as a warning to stop the fighting. The audience was greatly frightened. After the fight, it was discovered that the largest female tiger, named (Muxue), had been clawed in many places by her combative son (Shangjiao).

According to Ma Xishi, the tiger trainer, Muxue is actually very fierce. He recalled that two years ago in Vienna, Muxue gave birth to three cubs, but for some reason, she became ferocious and swallowed two of them. Shangjiao was rescued by Ma Xishi, who risked his life to reach into the tiger cage. According to reports, Muxue was carried on Ma's back during the performance on Monday night. When her son Shangjiao was walking into the cage, Muxue jumped at him, and the fierce fight began. Fortunately, it was stopped in time, and there were no major injuries.

Muxue has claw marks in many places and will not perform again until she has recovered. Ma Xishi is a beautiful and world-renowned tiger training master. His body has many claw and tooth marks from tigers, which shows how difficult it is to train tigers. Sai Huijun, the general manager of the circus, said that mother-son fights have occurred many times, and the audience does not need to panic, because the tiger cages in the circus are made of iron bars, and the tigers will definitely not escape and injure people during the fight.
