Naval Veteran Sa Zhenbing Arrives in Shanghai He is 73 Years Old and Comes to Discuss Hometown Disaster Relief and Stay with Relatives on Yuyuan Road 146

Naval veteran Sa Zhenbing has retired from his political career and lives at home, dedicating himself to disaster relief work. Previously, the Northern Warlord Zhang Yi burned and looted over a hundred villages in the Nangan area of Fuzhou, turning fields and houses into ruins. Sa Zhenbing personally traveled around, raising large sums of money, which not only restored the villages after the war but also provided infrastructure such as roads, bridges, and sanitation facilities that were unprecedented in any village. To this day, the 113 villages in the Nangan area regard Sa Zhenbing as a living Buddha. Since then, whenever there were floods or wars in Changle and Longyan counties, Sa Zhenbing single-handedly took responsibility for providing disaster relief. Even in remote areas with malaria and savage customs, Sa Zhenbing traveled alone without a single servant. Even in border areas infested with bandits, Sa Zhenbing, at the age of seventy, traveled among them. The bandits, moved by his sincerity in benefiting the people, respected him as a deity and did not harm him. Sa Zhenbing's lifestyle is like that of a farmer. He eats three meals a day, mostly wild vegetables and sweet potatoes provided by woodsmen and mountain people. His son, Fu Jun, serves as a director in the Ministry of Railways and has repeatedly invited him to live in the capital, but Sa Zhenbing always dismisses the idea with a smile, regarding the disaster-stricken areas as paradise and eating coarse food as delicacies. This year, he is 73 years old, but he is still energetic and walks briskly, looking like a man in his sixties. Recently, the communists captured northern Fujian, causing great suffering to the local area. Sa Zhenbing has once again appealed to various parties to raise funds for disaster relief. He happened to meet Hu Wenhu, a wealthy overseas Chinese businessman, in Fujian and personally visited him, urging him to donate money. Hu Wenhu also readily agreed. However, Fujian Province has suffered repeated disasters, and all the villages and cities are in ruins, making it very difficult to raise funds locally. Therefore, Sa Zhenbing arrived in Shanghai on the Wanxiang merchant ship the day before yesterday and is staying with relatives on Yuyuan Road. He will soon visit wealthy individuals to request donations for disaster relief in Fujian. After negotiating the details, he will return to Fujian to oversee everything.

Kong Xiangxi Returns to Shanghai Yesterday Morning 147

Kong Xiangxi, President of the Central Bank, flew from Shanghai to Beijing on a Sikorsky airplane a few days ago. Later, he traveled from Beijing to Jiangxi to report important matters to Chairman Jiang. He has now completed his task and returned to Beijing. After participating in the opening ceremony of the National Games, he took the night train back to Shanghai and arrived at the port at 8:00 AM yesterday. According to Kong, his trip to Beijing and Jiangxi was to report on the Central Bank's operations and to attend the National Day celebrations held by the National Government. There were no other special tasks.

British Textile Expert Parker Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday He is Hired as a Professor in the Textile Department of Jiaotong University The Local Textile Industry Will Prepare a Welcome 148

In response to the needs of society, the Ministry of Railways ordered the National

Jiaotong University to establish a textile department to train textile professionals and telegraphed Wang Jingchun, its representative in the United Kingdom, to hire Professor Parker, a renowned textile expert from the University of Leeds, as a professor in the university's textile department. Mr. Parker arrived in Shanghai yesterday by ship from England. Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University, sent personnel to welcome him at the wharf after receiving the news. At 4:00 PM, Mr. Parker, accompanied by his wife and son, visited the university. Li Zhaohuan, Zhong Weicheng, Qiu Weiyu, and others accompanied them on a tour of the entire campus and provided tea and snacks for them. Mr. Parker is currently staying at the Capital Hotel and plans to find a house near Xuhui in the future to prepare for all textile-related matters. It is reported that the local textile industry is preparing to welcome him.

Two Foreign Envoys Return to Shanghai Yesterday Belgian Envoy 149

The Belgian Ambassador to China, Mr. Jiumu, accompanied by his wife, took the night express train to Beijing on the evening of the 9th. He congratulated our authorities on National Day the day before yesterday. In the afternoon, he took the Beijing-Shanghai express train back from Beijing and arrived in Shanghai at about 11:00 PM last night. As the embassy in Beiping has urgent matters to attend to, the Belgian Ambassador is scheduled to return to the north on the 14th and return to Shanghai in about three months.

Japanese Envoy The Japanese Ambassador to China, Ariyoshi Akira, returned to Shanghai by train the night before last after traveling to Beijing to celebrate National Day, arriving at the port at 8:00 AM yesterday. He returned to his private residence to rest.

Pan Zhongjia, Magistrate of Shanghai County, Sworn in the Day Before Yesterday 150

Pan Zhongjia, Administrative Inspector of the Fifth District of Jiangsu Province and Magistrate of Shanghai County, took office on the 4th of this month and held a separate swearing-in ceremony. The Jiangsu Provincial Government appointed Jin Qian, Administrative Inspector of the 1st District and Magistrate of Songjiang County, as the oath supervisor. After receiving the appointment, Jin Qian arrived at the county government by car from Songjiang the day before yesterday. At 1:00 PM, a swearing-in ceremony was held in the auditorium. Members of the County Party Headquarters, the Education Bureau, the Property Office, the Technology Office, the Food Bureau, and the heads of various districts and public security bureaus under the county attended the ceremony. The presiding officer was Jin, the oath supervisor, and the recorder was Bi Huan. During the swearing-in ceremony, everyone stood in silence, sang songs, paid their respects to the Party and National Flag and the Premier's portrait, and listened respectfully to the Premier's last will. Then, Oath Supervisor Jin delivered a speech on behalf of the provincial government, followed by a speech by Oath-taker County Magistrate Pan. Next, Zhang Jingye, a member of the County Party Headquarters, delivered an encouragement speech. The ceremony then concluded.

Continued Hearing of the Case of Leaked Test Questions in the Shanghai Municipal Examination 151

During this year's Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Examination, leaked test questions were discovered. The Municipal Education Bureau transferred student Xie Ying and his brother Xie Zhen, as well as Zhang Jieliang, the head of the printing house, to the local court for investigation and prosecution by the prosecutor. After preliminary hearings, the court president appointed Chief of the Criminal Division Qian Chengjun to continue the hearings. Yesterday morning, the court reopened to continue the hearing. Xie Ying was released on bail but was absent due to illness. The judge questioned Zhu Zhenxun, who stated that he was 21 years old, from Anhui, and was formerly a member of the Testing Section of the Education Bureau. He currently resides at No. 5 Ruikang Lane, Dalin Road. He was asked about his relationship with Liu Jianan and replied that they were colleagues. He was asked how many people went to Nanjing to print the questions, and he replied that he and Liu Jianan went. He was asked who sealed the machine, and he replied that it was Director Pan. He was asked what subjects were in the questions, and he replied that there were high school, middle school, and elementary school questions. He was asked if there were Chinese, English, and math questions, and he replied that there were. He was asked who they hired to print the questions, and he replied that it was the Nanjing Printing House. He was asked who proofread the first time, and he replied that it was the printing house. He was asked what kind of paper was used, and he replied that it was very thin. He was asked when they did the proofreading, and he replied that it was the second time. He was asked what kind of paper it was, and he replied that it was the same as the first time. He said that they also proofread the third time and that it was on bond paper. He was asked when they first saw the proof, and he replied that it was on June 8th and that they were there from the 9th to the 11th. He was asked when they brought it back, and he replied that they took the night train home on the 11th. He was asked what sheets of paper were found, and he replied that he did not know, but that it was the test paper with the seal. At this point, the judge questioned Liu Jianan, who stated that he was 17 years old, from Xiangtan, and currently works in the Second Section of the Education Bureau, residing at No. 153 Huangjia Lane. He was asked when he and Zhu Zhenxun went to Nanjing, and he replied that they arrived at 3:00 PM on June 8th. He was asked how many questions they brought, and he replied that they brought one type of question. He was asked when he went to the Nanjing Printing House, and he replied that he went there on the 9th and started printing the next day. He was asked who proofread the first time, and he replied that it was the printing house. He was asked who proofread, and he replied that he did not know. He was asked when they did the proofreading, and he replied that it was the first and third times on the 9th and 10th and that they brought it back by night train on the 11th. He was asked what kind of paper they used to proofread the first time, and he replied that it was not the paper used to print the questions, but the proof paper. He was asked if the printed paper was the test paper, and he replied that it was. At this point, the judge questioned Xie Zhen, asking if the paper that Zhang Jieliang gave him was this sheet of paper. He replied that it was a separate copy. He was asked where the copy was, and he replied that it was lost. He was asked when he was paid, and he replied that it was on the 12th. He was asked if he still needed to make a copy even after he was paid on the 12th, and he replied that he did. He was asked why he said that it was printed when the prosecutor questioned him, and he replied that he did not say that. He was asked why he wanted to make a copy, and he replied that he did not understand some places and asked for an explanation. At this point, the judge questioned Zhang Jieliang, asking if he gave him the questions or made a copy. He replied that he did not make a copy. He was asked what he gave him, and he replied that it was English, life, and history. He was asked if he gave him the items that were found, and he replied that he did not. The judge said that the item was found by the prosecutor on the spot. At this point, the judge announced that the hearing would be continued at 2:00 PM on the 14th and adjourned the court.

Central Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Report 152

The 175th inspection report on the Central Bank's issuance reserve states that, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the bank's issuance of convertible notes. The 175th inspection was held at the bank's issuance bureau on October 9th, 1933. The inspection results are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 63,118,125 silver dollars, including 57,792,055 silver dollar notes and 5,329,770 fractional currency notes. The total amount of the reserve fund for convertible notes is 63,321,8125 silver dollars, including 51,824,125 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 47,794,181 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing vault, 2,082,675 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 1,798,569 silver dollars stored in fellow banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 11,394,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 416,715.4 customs gold units. The total amount of the reserve fund for customs gold convertible notes is 416,715.4 customs gold units, including 6,995.15 taels of bullion, which is equivalent to 416,715.4 customs gold units based on the fixed price of 59.57. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Regulations on Convertible Notes, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby made on October 11, 1933. Supervisors of the Central Bank: Chairman Li Fusun, Directors Xie Mingdong, Ju Songsun, Lan Qing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Hou, and Xu Jifei.

197th Report on Issuance Reserve of Four Banks Reserve 153

The Four Banks Reserve is jointly established by the Yanye, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks, and specializes in issuing banknotes of the Zhongnan Bank. According to the regulations for issuing from the reserve, the issuance of banknotes requires a 100% reserve, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guarantee reserve of no more than 40%. The announcement is made once a week and is audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 197th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve of October 7, 1932, is recorded as follows: the amount of banknotes in circulation is 23,997,537 yuan, the total amount of the reserve fund is 23,997,537 yuan, including a cash reserve of 19,200,5637 yuan and a guarantee reserve of 4,791,900 yuan.

Weather Report 155

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky here is cloudy, and Shandong and Binzhou will see northwesterly winds again. China's northern and northeastern areas will experience very strong seasonal winds, due to a low pressure system between Indochina and the island of Vitaya. The typhoon near Yabo is clearly moving rapidly to the northwest, with its center reaching within 120 miles of the intersection of 10 degrees north latitude and 135 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. In addition, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this port was a maximum of 75.2 and a minimum of 59.0. On the same day last year, the maximum was 75.7 and the minimum was 48.4.

Special Edition of the Shenbao National Games No. 3

Liu Changchun Equals Far Eastern Record in 100 Meters on Second Day of National Games National Records Swept Away Like Fallen Leaves in the Wind Ten New Men's and Women's Records Set in Two Days 156

On the second day of the National Games, the sky was overcast. Ticket sales began at various venues, resulting in a smaller audience than on the first day. However, all events except for the equestrian performance were held as scheduled, and the results were excellent. The national track and field records will be completely shaken. Liu Changchun's 100-meter race even equaled the Far Eastern record. Many other national records were broken. The details are recorded below.

Overcast Skies in Capital Yesterday Reduced Audience 157

(Nanjing, 11th) Ball games began at 8:00 AM on the 11th. The track and field semi-finals that were not completed on the afternoon of the 10th also began at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. The sky was overcast, with a slight glimpse of sunlight. Due to the impact of ticket purchases, the audience was not as large as in the morning. The large clock in the stadium stopped running. The entire lighting system for the National Games on the 10th suddenly went out. The audience yesterday afternoon was slightly larger than in the morning, but it was far less than that of the 10th.

Liu Changchun Equals Far Eastern Record in Men's 100-Meter Final His Time of 10.7 Seconds Breaks His Own National Record and Equals the Highest Record of the Far Eastern Games 158

(Nanjing, 11th) The men's 100-meter final was held at 3:00 PM on the 11th. Liu Changchun of Liaoning came in first, Han Jinglin of Hebei came in second, Cheng Jinguan of Shanghai came in third, and Hao Chunde of Shanghai came in fourth. The time of 10.7 seconds broke the national record and equaled the record held by Filipino Nepomuceno in the Far Eastern Games.

Liu Changchun of Liaoning 159

Seven New National Records Set in Men's and Women's Track and Field Finals Yesterday Men's 100 Meters, 1500 Meters, High Hurdles, Long Jump; Women's 50 Meters, 200 Meters, Javelin 160

(Nanjing, 11th) Yesterday afternoon's track and field finals were all exciting. The gathering of heroes, fierce competition, and intense interest were secondary to the continuous appearance of new national records. The old records were swept away like fallen leaves in the wind. Liu Changchun, a short-distance runner who attended the World Games, defeated heroes from the north and south in the 100-meter race, breaking his own national record of 10.8 seconds with a time of 10.7 seconds and equaling the Far Eastern record of Filipino Nepomuceno in the Far Eastern Games. This is truly a great achievement for China's track and field in modern times. Liu achieved this record after returning from the World Games, which can be said to be a benefit of this trip and also to comfort the people of the country. However, compared to the recent time of 10.4 seconds achieved by Japanese Yoshioka Takatoshi, there is still a gap. It is hoped that Liu will continue to work hard.

Women's 400-Meter Relay Preliminary Round

Guangdong Breaks National Record 168

55.2 seconds

(Nanjing, 11th) In the preliminary round of the women's 400-meter relay, the Guangdong team achieved a time of 55.2 seconds, breaking the national record. In the first group of the women's 400-meter relay preliminary round, the competitors were Guangdong, Shanghai, and Shandong. At the start, the Shanghai team took the lead, with Qian Hangsu running the first leg and Li Baohui running the second leg. In the third leg, at the handover to Li Yinan, the baton was delayed, and the Guangdong team overtook them. The Guangdong team set a new national record with a time of 55.1 seconds. The team members were Zhao Yunshan, Li Yuanfen, Zhang Jieqiong, and Chen Cuilan. In the first group, the participants were Henan, Nanjing, Qingdao, Hunan, Anhui, and Beiping. Qingdao took the lead all the way, but unfortunately, in the third leg, they dropped the baton and could not catch up. The Nanjing team won the championship. The team members were Hu Ruisheng, Liu Yulan, Yuan Chengliang, and Zhou Yueying. The results of the two groups are as follows: first group, Guangdong, Shanghai, Shandong, 55.2 seconds; second group, Nanjing, Henan, Beiping, 58.4 seconds.

Track and Field Finals: A Record of Heroes and Heroines – Liu Changchun's Astonishing Result in the 100-meter Final 169

In the 100-meter final, Liu Changchun won by a margin of ten meters. The final was a gathering of famous athletes and attracted considerable attention. It was the first event held on the afternoon of the eleventh. Spectators crowded at the finish line, and the press box was packed, with everyone focused intently. Guangdong's Zhong Lianji and Liaoning's Liu Changchun were the targets of the audience's gaze. Shanghai's Cheng Jinguan, Su Xiaoru, and others were also famous heroes of the time, all warming up on the field. Suddenly, the starting gun fired. In the crowd, it was difficult to discern who was in the lead initially, but after 50 meters, the athletes' abilities began to differentiate. Liu Changchun, like a horse freed from its reins, sprinted forward. Shanghai's Cheng Jinguan and Hebei's Zhao Jinglin followed closely. In the final stretch, Liu took the lead by five meters, achieving an astonishing time of 10.7 seconds, breaking his own national record of 10.8 seconds, which he had held for a year, and equaling the Far Eastern Games record. This was truly commendable. Guangdong's two leading athletes, Zhong Lianji and others, failed to qualify. Shanghai's Cheng and Hao came in third and fourth place respectively, while Su Xiaoru fell midway and was eliminated.

Creating a New National Record in the Women's Javelin Throw: (Shanghai) Chen Rongming

Lin Shaozhou Overwhelms All Rivals in the Hurdles 170

In the high hurdles final, Shanghai's star Chen Jiayou did not participate, missing the chance to compete against the best athletes from the north and south, which was quite regrettable. This event was full of talent. In the semi-finals on the morning of the eleventh, Hangzhou National Games high hurdles champion, Fujian's Lin Shaozhou, Guangdong's Huang Yingwei, and Shanghai's Nai Dinghua competed fiercely in the same group. Lin broke the national record with 16.4 seconds. Beijing's Liu Yingjun, Chen Ling from Shanghai, and Liu Renxiu from Liaoning were in the same group, making it even more exciting. Liu also broke the national record with 16.3 seconds. A fierce battle in the final was inevitable. It started in the afternoon, with eight athletes competing side by side in a line, each displaying good form, which was quite a sight to behold. Lin and Liu were the most competitive, remaining closely matched, making it difficult to determine who was ahead until the final sprint after the last hurdle. Lin was stronger, while Liu was weaker. Lin further shortened the new record he had set in the preliminary and semi-final rounds, creating an unprecedented great new national record with 16.2 seconds.

Zheng Sen Ultimately Wins the 1500 Meters 171

The 1500-meter final was a grand spectacle, held to the accompaniment of gentle music. In the first lap, Shanxi's Gu Desheng led, followed closely by Lu Daoxian, and Hebei's Zheng Sen. Shanghai's Dong Shuzhao was in third place, with the rest following in single file, forming a line. By the second lap, Dong Shuzhao had briefly taken the lead, but was soon overtaken by Peng Renbian. At this point, Zheng Sen was in fourth place, conserving his strength. In the final lap, in the last 500 meters, Zheng Sen truly surpassed the others, leading by five meters. Zhao Lianren moved into second place, while Dong Shuzhao was in third. In the last ten meters, Dong Shuzhao was overtaken by Shandong's Lü Changgeng, dropping to fourth. Zheng Sen's time was 4 minutes, 21.5 seconds, breaking the national record.

Guangdong Sweeps the Top Three Spots in the Women's 50 Meters 172

The women's 50-meter final was held after the men's 100 meters. The atmosphere was extremely tense. At the start, all the athletes were neck and neck, making it impossible to distinguish who was ahead. At the finish line, the differences were also minimal. Guangdong's Zhang Jieqiong, Li Yuanfen, and Zhao Yunshan swept the top three spots. Ping Landiqing came in fourth place, with a time of 6.9 seconds, breaking the national record. Shanghai's Li Baohui and Xiao Yingjie finished in seventh and eighth place, while Chen Shuqing was eliminated in the semi-finals.

Qian Hangsu Makes a Strong Comeback in the Women's 200 Meters 173

In the women's 200-meter final, Shanghai's Qian Hangsu, mindful of her poor performance in the preliminary round on the tenth, made a determined effort to improve and aimed to break the national record. As expected, she conserved her energy and made a stunning performance, creating an unprecedented time of 27.6 seconds, comparable to Liu Changchun's achievements. In the three groups of the semi-finals on the morning of the eleventh, all broke the national record. Beijing's Liu Yulan achieved 28.7 seconds, Shanghai's Qian Hangsu 27.9 seconds, and Shandong's Yu Xiulan 28.5 seconds. As for the championship in the final, there was no doubt that Qian would succeed. She further shortened her own time, making 27.6 seconds. This was extremely valuable. Yu Xiulan came in second, while Fujian's Xu Meiying, who lost to Qian in the semi-finals, came in fourth. Ping Jian Diqing, who lost to Yu in the semi-finals, came in third. Beijing's Liu Yulan, who came in first in the first group of the semi-finals, and Guangdong's Liu Youqing, who came in second, both failed to qualify in the final.

Quick Notes on Men's and Women's Field Events - Hao Chunde Makes a Stunning Performance in the Men's Long Jump 174

Hao Chunde made a stunning performance, creating a new long jump record with 6.912 meters. There were as many as 65 participants in the long jump competition, but 28 failed to show up. In the first jump, Shanghai's Hao Chunde and Wang Jihuai immediately set astonishing records of 6.912 meters and 6.73 meters, respectively, which were praised by representatives from other units. In the second jump, Jiangsu's Zhang Jiakui jumped 6.803 meters, breaking the national record along with Hao Chunde. There was not much improvement in the subsequent jumps. After three jumps, six athletes were selected for the final. Those who qualified were Jiangsu's Wang Hongjin, Zhang Jiakui, Shanghai's Hao Chunde, Wang Jihuai, Guangdong's Wang Wenxian, and Beijing's Liang... However, the outcome was already determined and difficult to change. After six jumps, the top three positions had already been decided. Hao Chunde is 29 years old this year, a student at Jinan University, and a sports star in Shanghai for the past five years. He won first place in the pentathlon and fourth place in the 100 meters at the last National Games. His performance was not outstanding. Later, Hao attended the Far Eastern Games but did not achieve much. In the past two years, Hao had not participated in any sports meet due to his declining performance. This year, Hao made a comeback at the Shanghai Municipal Games, winning the long jump and javelin throw. He then broke the long jump record at the National Games, demonstrating that Hao's ambition was not to be outdone by others. His stunning performance was commendable. If he can maintain this level, there is hope for the Far Eastern Games.

Lu Ming's Ambition to Succeed in the Men's Shot Put 175

Lu Ming's ambition was realized. Since participating in the 9th Far Eastern Games, Lu Ming had practiced diligently with the 16-pound shot put. He had also stated to reporters in Shanghai that he would achieve a result of over 12 meters at the next National Games. This time, he won the championship with 11.19 meters, demonstrating that ambition can lead to success. However, this result did not break the national record, which was disappointing. The reason for this lack of outstanding performance was due to the uneven ground and poor diet. If the ground had been smoother, Lu's result would have been around 11.50 meters.

Men's Discus Performance Greatly Disappointing 177

In the men's discus final, Zhang... achieved 34.84 meters, Leng Peigen from Beijing came in second with 34.48 meters, Gong Wan... came in third with 34.08 meters, and Liu Renxiu from Liaoning came in fourth with 32.29 meters. By the third throw, it had become... unrecognizable, making it difficult for the athletes. Athletes felt that it was unusually difficult, and many crossed the line. Chen Rongming Steadily Wins the Women's Javelin Throw 178

In the women's javelin final, Shanghai's famous thrower Chen Rongming's championship was as steady as Mount Tai. However, her performance was much worse than the Shanghai Municipal Games. Today, she won the championship with 26.38 meters, which was still far from the 27.75 meters at the Shanghai Municipal Games. The second and third place results both surpassed the old national record. Yu Liu Zhongwen came in second with 24.56 meters, Yu Yuan Hengrui came in third with 24.52 meters, and Min Chen Rongtang came in fourth with 21.155 meters.

This was the first women's javelin event in the National Games, so the number of participants from various units was not large, totaling only 39 people, and many were absent. Most of the running and throwing postures were not correct. Shanghai's Chen Rongming is a well-known figure in women's basketball. Her height, strength, and power are rare among women. Therefore, in the first throw, she achieved 26.38 meters, leaving the women from the other 22 units far behind. After three throws, six athletes were selected for the final: Li Shufang (Guangzhou), Chen Rongming (Shanghai), Gan Hongying (Shanghai), Liu Zhongwen (Henan), Yuan Hengrui (Henan), and Chen Rongtang (Fujian). As a result, Chen Rongming (Shanghai) won the championship with 26.38 meters.

Zou Shande's Unexpected Victory in the Women's High Jump 179

Shandong's Zhu Tianzhen, who held the national record of 1.255 meters, was expected to win the championship, but not only did she fail to win, she did not even place. Shanghai's high jump champion, Zou Shande, won the championship with 1.28 meters, greatly improving her own performance. Wang Huachang from Shanghai also came in second. Zou's vaulting posture was excellent, unmatched in the entire venue, and she could be trained in the straddle technique. However, her straight jump was still lacking. It was a pity that Ji Wang Shuzhen, one of the last seven or eight people, ducked back under the bar after jumping over it, resulting in a foul. Despite repeated attempts, she failed to clear the bar and was eliminated. Zhu Dazhen's body was overweight, making her jumps less agile, which led to her elimination. When the bar was at 1.24 meters, there were still four athletes left, two from Shanghai and two from Guangdong. When the bar was raised to 1.28 meters, the two women from Guangdong failed to clear it, while Zou and Wang both cleared it, competing for the top spot. Zou eventually won the championship. After the rankings were determined, Zou raised the bar again to try for a higher jump, but was unsuccessful. It was an unexpected success for Shanghai to win the first and second place in this event. Before the women's high jump, Ms. Zhang Huilan led the referees to inspect the field and check the high jump stands. The take-off area was 1.04 meters, with one side higher and one side lower. According to the women's high jump rules, the take-off area should be 914 meters. Attempts to find the person in charge of the venue were unsuccessful. The referees had to find carpenters to drill holes, which delayed the competition by more than 20 minutes. This must be attributed to the negligence of the venue management. At the roll call, 20 people were absent, with only 28 present. Overall, Guangdong's Liang Qianhua had the best posture, followed by Jiangsu's Hui Lanwei. None of the others were correct. Shandong's Zhu Dazhen, who had the highest hopes of winning, had gained weight and could no longer be as agile as a swallow, breaking the women's high jump record. When the high jump reached... meters...4, Ms. Zhu and the others were eliminated at the same time. Only four athletes cleared the bar, evenly split between Guangdong and Shanghai. As a result, Shanghai's Zou Shande won the high jump championship with a score of 1.208 meters, defeating the female athletes from thirty-two units. However, the results were slightly worse than in the past.

Shanghai Wins Over Fujian 7-0

Four Goals in the First Half, Three Goals in the Second Half

In the third soccer match, Shanghai defeated Fujian 7-0. It was held at 4:00 PM, with Chen Jixiang as the referee. It was Shanghai's first match, and due to their great reputation, many people came to watch. The Fujian team was mostly composed of young men under 20 years old, who were lively and brave, and their strength was quite strong. At the beginning of the match, the Fujian team was quite nervous. Within five minutes, Li Yichen scored the first goal. Three minutes later, Sun Jinying got the ball and passed it to Wan Xianghua, who kicked it accurately, and the ball flew in again. By the 15th minute, Li Yichen scored another goal. At this point, the Fujian team began to rally slightly, resisting desperately and fighting their way through. Fortunately, Zhou Xianyan's iron gate was as solid as a mountain, successfully saving dangerous shots. After a fierce battle for 20 minutes, Sun Jinshun scored another goal. The first half ended with Shanghai leading 4-0. In the second half, Shanghai's Chen Hongguang replaced Li Yichen, and Luo Haiguang replaced Chen Jiaqiu. After 25 minutes of intense fighting, Sun Jinshun opened the scoring. Chen Hongguang followed suit. Finally, Tu Kaiyuan scored a long-range shot. The second half ended with Shanghai winning 3-0. The overall score was 7-0, with Shanghai winning. The Fujian team had excellent spirit, and their skills were also commendable. It was unfortunate that they met a strong opponent in the first round.

Women's Softball: Shanghai Wins its First Match Against Henan 185

At 9:00 AM on the 11th, the women's softball match between Shanghai and Henan was held on the track and field. The Shanghai team was organized by Southeast and East Asia. After the Shanghai Municipal Games, they trained diligently, and their skills were quite remarkable. Their batting and fielding were both excellent. The Henan team was disorganized and made many mistakes in the field. As a result, Shanghai won the game by 27-2 in seven innings. The referees were Wu Bangwei and Hou Shexun, and the scorekeeper was Ma Xunbo.

▲Two Home Runs

In the second inning, Shanghai's Zeng Huiqiong hit a home run. In the top of the fourth inning, Pan Yueying also hit a home run. The ball landed and bounced quickly out of the center field. Also, in the second inning, Shanghai's first baseman, Li Baofan, caught a pop fly. Henan's Zhou Fanglu, who was originally on first base, tried to advance to second base. Li immediately threw the ball to the shortstop, Sun now at first base, who caught it, resulting in a double play. This was a highlight of the match.

▲Shanghai's Pitching and Hitting are Excellent

Shanghai's pitcher, Zou Shande, pitched well with excellent technique. In seven innings, she never gave up four balls. She only struck out three times. Henan's pitcher, Yuan Rui, is a famous track and field and softball thrower, but her pitching skills were poor. Her pitches were soft and slow, and the Shanghai team often scored four balls twice and struck out three times. Shanghai's batting skills were also impressive. The catcher, Pan Yueying, was also more stable and experienced than Henan's Chen Rui. ▲Overview of the Game

Shanghai batted first and started strongly, scoring eight runs in the first inning, with Sun, Li, Meng, Zeng, Pan, and Lu scoring. Henan was completely overwhelmed. In the second inning, Xiang Shaoliang's high ball was caught, and Meng occupied first base. Zeng Huiqiong hit a home run, scoring two points. Henan scored one point with Liu Lixue. In the third inning, Shanghai scored five more points, with Xu Chang and Sun Jieren running back. Henan made no progress due to Shanghai's fielding and passing. In the fourth inning, Shanghai scored eight more points, with Ren, Xu, Lu, Sun, Xiang, Sun, Zeng, and Pan scoring. Pan Yueying's home run contributed greatly to this inning, scoring two points in a row. Henan scored zero. In the fifth, sixth, and seventh innings, Shanghai made slight adjustments to their lineup and only scored four points. Henan only scored one point in the fifth inning. In total, Shanghai won 27-2.

Anhui was helpless, unable to advance or retreat. The Beiping team was like a raging fire, winning the fourth quarter 26-0. In conclusion, Beiping won 71-8. The referee was Shu.

Criticism of the Central Sports Field Building 199

— Wu Yunrui

Before I start writing, the first thing I want to declare is that I do not know the designer and have no prejudice against him. However, for the sake of academic research, I must criticize him. If there are any inappropriate points, please forgive the architect. This field is too far from the city. Now, everyone who comes to visit the field criticizes it. In fact, when the author designed and built it three years ago, he published opinions against it in the newspaper. Those who paid attention to it should still remember it. At that time, the September 18th Incident had not yet occurred, and the national situation was better. The government had a plan to build government office buildings next to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. Building south of the mausoleum was indeed a far-reaching plan. Unexpectedly, the war between the government and the warlords greatly damaged the country's vitality. Due to the September 18th Incident, the government's plan to build next to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum could not be realized. As a result, a great sports field had to be isolated in front of the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. This was caused by the situation, not the responsibility of the government authorities, nor the responsibility of the architect. Now that the die is cast, there is no need to blame too much for the inconvenience of being too far from the city. During the preparation period for this National Games, the author, as the deputy director-general, also served as the head of the venue equipment section, and went to the field to inspect and supervise the work for more than a month. Therefore, regarding the advantages and disadvantages of the field and the experience gained from studying sports buildings and equipment over the years, there are many things that I cannot help but say. I will discuss them in detail.

Track and Field 200

1. The Area Occupied by the Stands is Too Large

The purpose of the stands is to enable visitors to see various sports clearly. If you sit on the stands and cannot see the various sports clearly, then the stands are useless. If the running track is more than 600 meters, then people on the stands cannot see various sports clearly. Therefore, some people advocate building an 800-meter running track, but they do not understand this. The running track of the Central Sports Field is 500 meters, which is already not small (usually 400 meters). Even if the stands are built close to the running track, it is still not possible to see all the items in the field clearly. Now, four basketball (or volleyball courts) are set up outside the ends of the curved sections of the running track. As a result, the people sitting on the stands in the two curved sections cannot see the track and field events clearly. The stands in the two curved sections are the same as being empty for track and field events, which is too uneconomical. Moreover, basketball courts and volleyball courts have their own specialized buildings outside the track and field. Of the eight courts in the curved section of the stands, only one was used this time. The other eight courts are the same as being empty. Most of the cost of building a track and field goes to the stands. Now, because useless ball courts are built inside the stands, a large amount of money is spent on useless stands, wasting national funds. It is a pity that the architect had already left the capital to go to Shenyang when this field was built. Otherwise, when the plan was first set, I would have criticized it greatly in the newspaper and hoped to save the country's expenses.

2. The Running Track is Too Wide, Whether Straight or Curved. According to Dr. Diem, a German expert in sports architecture, the straight section of the running track should be 7.2 meters (six lanes, 1.2 meters per lane). Because the results of the 100-meter and 200-meter races are improving every day, the difference between first and second, and second and third, may be within one or two centimeters in the future. If too many people run together, it will be very difficult for the finish line referee. The northern ends of the straight and curved sections of the Central Sports Field are all 15 meters. This width can accommodate 12 people running together. The designer probably thought that this wide track could allow 12 people to run in the 100-meter, 200-meter, 400-meter, and 400-meter hurdles, saving the number of preliminary and semi-final runs. I don't know that saving the number of preliminary and semi-final runs is one thing, and judging is another thing. Taking the 400-meter hurdles as an example, one inspector probably watches one or two rows. If there are twelve hurdles in one row, then the twelve jumpers will come one after another. It is not easy to see who fouls. The hurdles in the curved section are uneven, and the more hurdles there are, the wider the field of vision, and the more difficult it is to see who fouls. Moreover, according to the latest rules, if a foot or leg slightly hits a hurdle and it shakes, it is considered a knockdown. The judge must be even more astute. If there are twelve people running together, it will be difficult for the inspector to see clearly. Therefore, a 15-meter running track is inevitably too wide. Because the running track is wide, the scope of the stands cannot be small, and the construction costs money again. Therefore, from the perspective of the running track, it also makes the construction uneconomical.

3. All the Jumping Tracks and Running Tracks in the Entire Field are Lower Than the Ground on Both Sides, Which is a Major Mistake in Construction. The most important things in a track and field are the running track and the jumping track, and the most important thing to pay attention to in construction is the drainage problem on the track. Because the water on the running track and the jumping track can quickly drain away after the rain, the weather can clear and the movement can continue. Now, the jumping tracks and running tracks in the Central Sports Field are all lower than the ground on both sides. As a result, all the water gathers on the jumping track and the running track when it rains, which is a big mistake. Now, the mouths of the drainage holes are all lower than the running track. I don't know what the designer's intention is. I cannot understand it.

4. The Location of the Track and Field Items in the Field is Not Legal.

According to the legal configuration, the iron ring for the discus throw in the field competition is placed in the center of the curved section of the running track. Because the direction of the discus throw can be fired in all directions within 180 degrees, even experienced veterans will occasionally release the discus and shoot horizontally. If the discus circle is not placed in the center but is placed on the side of the curved section, there is a danger of the discus throwing into the kneeling track. Now, a high jump area is set up in the center of the southern curved section, occupying the position of the discus, and the discus has to be set on the side close to the running track, which is full of dangers and can be expected. On the one hand, the distance of the run-up during the high jump is not large, and the fan-shaped jumping track can be placed on both sides of the curved section. Now, it is placed in the center, hindering the position of the discus, which can be said to be no planning at all.

5. The Sand Pit is Too Deep and Too Short, and the Jumping Track for the Triple Jump is Too Short. The Sand Surface in the Sand Pit is Uneven with the Take-Off Board.

The sand pit should not be too deep. If it is too deep, the jumper will flow down too much when he falls into the pit, and the loss of performance will be great. Therefore, the depth of the sand pit should be from two feet to two and a half feet. If the long jump pit is too short, the jumpers will be wary, which will reduce the performance. The triple jump track is more than 45 meters from the sand pit. Now, all that is available in this field is about 35 meters. Subtracting the distance of more than 11 meters between the take-off board and the sand pit, there are only about 25 meters left. Within this distance, it is impossible to make the jumping runner increase the speed to the maximum extent. Therefore, before the meeting, the jumping track was lengthened by 10 meters. The original sand surface in the sand pit was lower than the jumping track by more than four or five inches, which is related to the performance. The lower the sand surface in the sand pit, the higher the performance jumped than it should be. The more the sand surface is higher than the jumping track, the lower the performance jumped than it should be. If the sand surface is too high or too low, it is enough to make the performance inaccurate. The wooden edges around the sand pit this time were originally too low, and they were all raised by four or five inches to make the sand surface also rise by four or five inches.

In addition to the above shortcomings, there are others, such as the baseball field being too small, the football field having no way out, and there being no gap between the stands and the field. Due to the limitation of space, I cannot evaluate them in detail. I hope that the designing gentlemen will refer to Chinese and foreign sports architecture books more in the future, so that the same mistakes will not be discovered in other fields.

National Games Male and Female Athletes Should Pay Attention to Sports Medicine 214

(Part 1)

Athletes' Physique Changes and Physical Strength Improvement 215

Sports can improve health, promote the development of internal organs, and create a good physique. A healthy person with an excellent physique does not necessarily have sufficient physical strength to win in sports competitions. The physique we need is a typical healthy physique, not a strongman's physique. Therefore, the win-loss rate in sports competitions cannot be used to judge whether a person's physique is healthy. In theory, physical strength and health are two different issues. Health needs exercise to improve it, and muscles and the heart become stronger, and physical strength gradually increases. However, to improve health through exercise, it must be done through long-term training. An athlete's physical strength can improve significantly after several weeks or months of training. This is not due to the development of muscles and internal organs, but a representation of the improvement in sports records. After a long period of training, the athlete's original physique will transform into an altered physique. Due to the change in physique, physical strength is abnormally increased. In the 1913 All-European Rowing Competition held in Germany, the pulse of the winning German athlete Graf was only 54 beats per minute after the race, while other athletes exceeded 100 beats per minute. After fierce competition, his pulse was even lower than that of a normal person at rest. This proves the change in his physique. Athletes with altered physiques can often produce excellent physical strength.

Special Heart Images of Athletes at the Finish Line of the 50-meter Preliminary Are a Sign of Physical Alteration 216

An athlete's heart is generally too large in diameter. This can be clearly demonstrated during diagnosis. A heart that is not large in diameter must be too small, but it is less common than a normal heart. A heart that is too large in diameter is called an "athlete's heart." The so-called "athlete's heart" has been studied by medical experts around the world for 30 years. Regarding the results of the research, there are various different reports. According to the opinions of most researchers, people with "athlete's heart" have better physical strength than normal people. This "athlete's heart" hypertrophy is different from other pathological heart hypertrophy. According to the research of Dr. Bergseiva of Germany, bicycle athletes account for the largest number of athletes with hypertrophic hearts in Germany, followed by sledding, marathon running, swimming, and fighting athletes. According to the research of Dr. Goff of Austria, the hearts of rowing, cycling, and sledding athletes are the largest, the hearts of swimming, mountaineering, and weightlifting athletes are average, and the hearts of football and fencing athletes are the smallest. Moreover, the shapes are also very different from normal people. The size of athletes' hearts varies depending on the sport. For example, the heart contours of fencing athletes are divided into teardrop-shaped hearts, spherical hearts, relaxed hearts, acute-angled hearts, and pointed hearts. The changes in an athlete's heart vary with the number of days of training. The hearts of those with minor changes can return to their original state in a short period of time after stopping exercise. Once they stop exercising, their health will gradually decline, but their physical strength will increase compared to before.

Athletes' Low Blood Pressure, Slow Breathing, and Urine Abnormalities 217

Athletes' blood pressure is mostly low. This is closely related to the "athlete's heart" mentioned in the previous section. However, some ordinary athletes sometimes have higher blood pressure than normal people. Low blood pressure is a sign of physically excellent athletes. In these athletes, the pulse gradually decreases during exercise, and the heart's strength also decreases. Therefore, athletes breathe less often at rest than normal people. Normal people breathe 13 to 20 times per minute. Anything less than that is called "slow breathing." Breathing is linked to the pulse. When the pulse is slow, breathing is also slow. With fewer breaths, they can achieve better results during exercise. The breathing rate of an athlete with slow breathing does not increase more than that of a normal person during exercise. In summary, the signs of low blood pressure and slow breathing are proof of physical alteration. Athletes exhibit these effects when their physical strength improves.

After excessive exercise, urine abnormalities are a well-known fact. This is due to acute nephritis. The physical alteration of trained athletes has been described above, so the condition of their blood also changes, making it easier to mimic the function of the kidneys. After strenuous exercise, they will find abnormalities in their urine composition, especially in trained athletes. This is also a sign of physical alteration.

Functional Changes in the Nervous System Are Divided into Physiological and Pathological 218

The number of heartbeats (i.e., pulse) and contraction force and tension are often controlled and regulated by the sympathetic and parasympathetic nerves. In other words, the parasympathetic nerve has an inhibitory effect on heartbeats, while the sympathetic nerve has a promoting effect on the heart. If the function of the parasympathetic nerve is superior to the function of the sympathetic nerve, the number of heartbeats will decrease. The slowness of an athlete's pulse is due to the oversensitivity of the parasympathetic nerve, which praises the relaxation of their heart muscle. With a relaxed heart, the volume also expands. The cause of the "athlete's heart" is the lack of tension in the heart muscle and the return to the oversensitivity of the parasympathetic nerve. The low blood pressure of athletes is also caused by the oversensitivity of the parasympathetic nerve. An adult with a pulse rate of more than 80 beats per minute is considered to have a fast pulse. Athletes also use this standard for a fast pulse. However, among 70 martial artists, there are at most only three with fast pulses. The neurological alteration can also be demonstrated by abnormal reflexes and facial nerves. Exercise training can not only cause changes in the parasympathetic nerve, but also alter all nervous systems. However, the parasympathetic nerve is the main sign of proving physical alteration. From this point of view, if the changes in the nervous system function of an athlete can adapt to a certain sport and are similar to the standards of normal people, then the changes are physiological phenomena. If the changes reach the highest degree and physical strength declines as a result, then it is completely a pathological convulsion. Therefore, when discussing the changes in the nervous system function of athletes, it is important to pay attention to the two types of distinctions: physiological and pathological.

Disease Due to Overwork and Mild to Severe Physical Alteration 219

If exercise training is too intense, it is easy to get sick due to physical alteration, which hinders the health of the body. This is the so-called overtraining. There are many people who have lost their lives due to illness. However, the reversal of the healthy state of athletes is not accidental. In the middle of exercise training, the physique gradually turns in the direction of alteration. People blindly believe that exercise can improve health, but they do not know that athletes who get sick or even die from exercise are endless. This lovely phenomenon must be explained once. Sports exercise is not as great as we idealize it to be in improving health. It can only change the physique. Depending on the appropriate training method, athletic ability will improve accordingly. The extent to which exercise training should alter the physique is also a matter for discussion. If exercise training is too intense, it can change the athlete's innate physique, the quality of the nervous system, and the heart's congenital adaptability (hereditary endocrine function). When athletes reach their highest records, they must undergo intense training, so their physical alteration has almost reached its extreme. During overtraining, the body is prone to fatigue, which can easily lead to diseases and a lot of danger. In summary, when the body is mildly altered, athletic ability can also reach an excellent point. On the other hand, severe alteration can easily lead to disease. Therefore, athletes must use diagnosis to distinguish the degree of physical alteration and take strict precautions regarding the measurement of exercise training.

Athletes Who Do Not Feel Fatigue Have Blood and Acidic Products Harmonized 220

During exercise, the body's metabolism is very vigorous. The waste products such as carbon dioxide, lactic acid, and phosphoric acid produced by the body are more than usual (at rest). Under normal circumstances, these acidic products are mixed with proteins, bicarbonates, and phosphates in the blood. The body's chemistry and reactivity can constantly maintain the body's health and maintain a state of equilibrium. However, during exercise, the amount of these acidic products increases sharply, and the blood gradually loses its ability to mix with them. This is a major cause of physical fatigue. Especially when a large amount of lactic acid is produced, the ability of carbon dioxide to harmonize with the blood decreases significantly. This is because the blood's reserve capacity is weak. However, people who have undergone considerable physical training have the possibility of gradually increasing the carbon dioxide in their blood. Athletes who have undergone considerable training have more blood production during exercise than normal people, which is sufficient to harmonize with acidic products. Therefore, trained athletes do not feel fatigued even after prolonged exercise. This state of blood change is entirely due to regular exercise training. It is naturally easier for these athletes to improve their performance. However, the special blood changes in athletes are more closely related to their physical alteration. Overtraining easily leads to disorders of the nervous system and hypersensitivity of the parasympathetic nerve.

Random Talk on Architecture by Lin Huiyin 221

Chinese people are the most progressive people and the people who are most likely to achieve complete success in everything. For example, taking architecture as an example, it has not been long since it transitioned from the old method to the new method, but it has easily reached its highest point and has already made people feel tired of it.

Since you are tired of it, you cannot seek some new stimulation. You feel that the old architecture is really good, it looks pleasing to the eye, and it is leisurely to live in, but you cannot say it out loud, because you are afraid that people will say that you are going backwards. So you say in a roundabout way... the old architecture should indeed be abolished. But the glazed tiles are worth preserving. In fact, you know that there are many reinforced concrete buildings that use glazed tiles, but no one has ever advocated that... you advocated that, so that people can see the combination of the two new materials, and they will think of it as being achieved by your suggestion. And in your heart, you will still have a sincere hope, hoping that the reinforced concrete and cement under the glazed tiles will still be replaced with earth bricks and lime.

Or you think that the reason why new architecture needs to be built meticulously and delicately is only to demonstrate to the old architecture, which means that the new architecture can also do what the old architecture can do, because the old architecture is very meticulous and very delicate. But you feel that the demonstration period has passed, and you believe that the new architecture is already meticulous enough and delicate enough, and should no longer continue to be so meticulous and delicate. And what is needed now should be knives and guns. The whole city is brutal. There are bombs everywhere. As long as you touch it slightly, you will be in danger of being bombed to death. Otherwise, the meticulous and delicate architecture will be dangerous. Because it will be麻醉性的. You will be麻醉性d to death without even knowing it. When you see all this, you can't bear it anymore and issue a warning to change the new architecture to a new direction.

Chinese people are the most progressive people, and it can be foreseen that a newer architecture will be completed soon.

National Sickness by Gao Zhi 222

Since I have been sick in bed, and I have been getting headaches from Chinese doctors and Chinese medicine every day, I have been thinking wildly in silence, and I seem to have realized something. People's bodies can get sick, and countries can also get sick. China has been called the "Sick Man of East Asia," and there is no doubt that it is sick. If a country is sick, then the disease should be called national sickness.

What exactly is China's national sickness? I will not make a conclusion here, but just say my personal opinion. Some say that the national sickness is laziness, or that the national sickness is the aging of the nation, but these seem too abstract. China is founded on agriculture, and officials are truly lazy, but the farmers are considered to be the most diligent. From a biological point of view, the nation will not age.

According to those who are engaged in the civil education movement in Dingxian, the four major diseases of the Chinese people (that is, China) are ignorance, poverty, weakness, and selfishness. This means that more than 80% of the national population is illiterate, some are so poor that they do not even have food to eat, and they are not strong, do not know hygiene, and there is no civic training at all. Everyone only knows selfishness and does not know public interest.

Since the Xinhai Revolution, there have been twenty-two years. Regarding "ignorance," isn't there a Ministry of Education there to educate the people? Regarding "weakness," the Ministry of Health (Department) has been established for many years, and the country is promoting it very enthusiastically. Soon everyone will be strong, not addicted to opium, and can also practice meditation to temper their spirits and pray for the country to eliminate disasters. As for poverty, hasn't the government issued hundreds of millions of internal and external debts? It is doing construction projects, and the cotton and wheat loans are coming again, and what treasury bonds are going to be issued, and there are also aviation lottery tickets, giving everyone the opportunity to win 500,000 yuan. The government only takes half of the total income. But have these monies cured the four diseases?

This again involves the issue of "selfishness." The selfishness of the general public for food and clothing does not count as a disease. The selfishness of those who are "public servants" of the general public is the real disease. The strength or weakness of the national system certainly depends on the level of the people's power, but the leadership and responsibility of the leaders are the prerequisites for prosperity and decline. What was Japan like before the Meiji Restoration? What were Italy and Germany like before the 1860s? What has the Soviet Union become in fifteen years? What was it like before? A leader who blames all the bad things on the people is incompetent and shameful. However, the leaders have power, and with power they can act selfishly. If a high official or a big warlord acts selfishly, hundreds of thousands or millions of people will die of poverty and starvation. Public debts, internal debts, treasury bonds, etc. are increasing, the people are suffering more and more, and the national sickness is becoming more and more difficult to improve. Maybe this is the national sickness?

When people are sick, there are still Chinese medicine and medicine to deal with them. When the country is sick, what should be done?

Sequel to Rectifying Books by Tang Tao 223

Suddenly, a thought flew into my mind, "Rectifying Books!"

But it is really difficult. Inside these books, there are His Majesty the Emperor, revolutionary martyrs, and poets, all of whom are present. Rectifying them is a very troublesome thing. If I cite the ceremonial system of the previous dynasty, it would have been treason a few years ago, and now it is a traitor to the Japanese, a double crime, not to be trifled with! But if I do not wear a hat or shoes, or put on the mask of a gentleman or an old fox, and do it casually, the poet will say... (This is just a supporting role!)

In the past, I also followed the second elder, entered and exited the gate of sages, and traveled around the land of poetry and propriety, listening to them praise the Six Classics and advocate the Eight Virtues, holding the late emperor as high as the sky, and I was very unhappy in my heart! Later, I was moved by Lao Tzu and Zhuang Zhou, and felt that everything would be empty in the end. I wanted to ride a green ox out of the Hangu Pass.

But in the end, I did not succeed.

This is a good thing for people who love good articles. Because if I really became an immortal, the gentlemen would have lost an object to slander, and famous articles would have been buried, wouldn't that be a pity!

From then on, I decided not to read the Tao Te Ching and Zhuangzi, and put them in the fold of the bookshelf.

But the essays and short stories of the Jin Dynasty are what I have loved all my life... The reason is that when I read them aloud, I always feel fresh and delightful. I would never feel like the modern popular "Road Pilgrimage" or "XX Symphony," that I have to take aspirin while reading!

The old shopkeeper of the pharmacy is so energetic because the fake and shoddy goods are so great.

Next to the essays of the Jin Dynasty, I put the Yuan opera.

Next are more than a dozen complete collections. Inside there is "XX Prose," which is said to be the legacy of a sage. A half-life monkey, a hundred-year-old crown dog, alas!

I put the new and old poems and lyrics together. The new ones have not been tried, and the old ones? This tune has not been played for a long time. Anyway, in ancient times there were talented scholars and beautiful women, and now there are young masters. They will make friends themselves, so I will not say more.

There are the most novels in each book, especially the foreign texts that crawl like crabs. I will rectify them one by one. Originally, I wanted to say a few words, but it is said that the best articles are written concisely, and it is especially strictly forbidden to touch other people's sore spots.

Let's stop here. And I wish that the world will have the same writing system and not suffer from hysterical diseases!

Ganpu Correspondence (3) by A Ying 224

Brother ○○:

Due to special reasons, I returned to Shanghai on the 18th and came to Ganpu for the second time on the 20th. The matter has not been completely settled, and it is still impossible to go to the salt folk immediately. Feeling bored, the elegance of the literati arose, and we gathered a few people to go hiking. At this time, I also became a literati, which is really like the advertisement for Bai Lingji, a bit unexpected. However, I did become a literati. I will report this day's elegance to you as a digression in "Ganpu Correspondence."

This time, there were five people in total, including me. We set off from Wancang Mountain, where we lived, at 10:30 a.m., passed Dahu Mountain, where there were many pine trees. There was a stone bridge and a stream at the foot of the mountain. The rice had turned yellow and the fragrance was intoxicating. We walked west along the stream to the tomb of Zhu Rui, the governor of Zhejiang in the early Republic of China. The beard of one of the stone figures had the flavor of a Ren Dan beard. From this, it can be seen that living people like to be linked to Japan, and even the dead are proud to be associated with Japan, which is very sad. Behind the tomb is Zhu An, built over the stream. The stream flows horizontally in front of the main hall. It must be very majestic after heavy rain, but unfortunately it is now dry, as if the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted. There is a bridge over the stream that leads directly to the main hall. I am not a Buddhist disciple, so I do not know who is enshrined there. We sat by the cave to drink tea and looked at the grape trellis built by the stream and the ivy along the house, red flowers. A poetic inspiration was a bit eruptive, but when I thought of the grapes planted by my father in my hometown seven years ago, and the sad mood when Mr. Zhu Fu wrote "Ivy Walk," my poetic mood was sent down to the eighteenth level of hell. However, let us have Xu Zhimo continue to monopolize the patent.

At 11:10, we left Zhu An and went up Daqi Mountain along the stream. We climbed about 400 steps on stone steps to Xu Zhonglie's tomb, which was not yet finished. I closed my eyes and meditated, thinking that it would be a great sight to see the mountain torrents surging and the water splashing here after heavy rain. I deeply cursed the old sky for not having a torrential rain yesterday. Looking at the spirit tablet, I learned that this Xu Zhonglie (named Yongyi, styled Jifu, and nicknamed Xiaoyun, from Haiyan) was an anti-imperialist in the Gengzi year, and he was killed for being anti-imperialist. I thought that the establishment of this tomb was much more meaningful than Zhu's tomb. No wonder there was no Ren Dan beard or the upturned beard often seen in movies on the mouth of the stone figure in front of his tomb. We stood in awe and looked at it for a long time. Afterwards, we passed through Shanzhen Village, crossed Lu Jialing, and arrived at the bamboo forest at the foot of the ridge. The sun had already made my head hurt, but suddenly I found a bamboo forest with ten thousand poles. Walking inside, it was really cool and comfortable, and there was the sound of Xiao Xiao's music. Going up, it is Tanxian Ridge. It is said that the stone road along the way was built by Tanxian overnight, and there are gold nuggets under the stones. Dreaming of getting rich is already ridiculous. It is even more peculiar to know that there is gold but not to dig it, but just talk about it. Fortunately, heaven and earth know that I do not want to get rich, so I will not criticize his mother. There is also a stream along the mountain, and there is a protruding round concave in the stream. It is said that this is the place where Tanxian bathed. Even if the water is cut off above and below, this place will never be exhausted, and the water can cure sores, which people can testify. It is natural that there is sulfur in the water that can cure sores. It is indeed a strange coincidence that it will never be exhausted all year round. Therefore, after this day's trip was over, I made an appointment with two friends to run to take a bath. This bath was indeed more pleasant than the hot springs in Shanghai. The regret is that the water that never runs dry in this natural bathtub was emptied by the efforts of our three people in less than ten minutes... The two friends were still not reconciled and used towels to wipe up even the remaining drops. If Tanxian knew, I think he would definitely shout unlucky! The relics of the immortals also have the opportunity to be stripped bare. Thinking of this, I couldn't help but feel happy! But my correspondence had to end in the middle of this "happiness." Brother ○○, let's talk again tomorrow.

A Ying, Evening of August 21

Preface to Lushan Zhi by Zhang Taiyan 225

My friend Wu Zongci Ailin compiled the twelve volumes of Lushan Zhi. Yining Chen Shu preface it. The catalog is detailed. He asked me for a preface again. I said: "The ancient Lushan housed hermits and accommodated monks. The present Lushan is full of tigers and wolves and built with magnificent houses. There are dozens of famous mountains in China, from Mount Wutai to Zhongnan, Qingcheng, Diancang, and Emei. Huangshan and Kuocang are nearby. The land is either remote or on the main road, and ships cannot reach it. Only Lushan, backed by the Yangtze River, is easily accessible to foreigners and laymen. Those who want to hide in this place are indeed due to the terrain. However, from now on, the mountains will be more densely wooded and the markets will be more expansive. Those who want to hide in this place must be highly moralistic to be able to remember themselves. It is not sad if one cannot obtain what one seeks. However, is it not the greatest sorrow in the world to seek seclusion but not find a place to escape? Ailin is a man of the world, who has been walking north and south as a member of parliament for decades. He left because he could not speak out. Since then, he has not been subdued by injustice. He often lives in this mountain, hoping to stay away from madness and self-respect. The records he made in the Zhi are detailed about the ancient scenic spots and the changes in the present. The chapter on mountain politics is especially factual and can be used to prepare stories. The appropriateness of his feelings is not unknowable. In short, the Lushan of today is somewhat far from what Ailin expected. I now know that Heaven's encouragement of things is indeed not the same as the love and joy of sages." I wrote this on the title page. September of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Zhang Binglin.

A Page of Love! Hurry up! Otherwise, your love will be cold! 226

"The potatoes are a bit smelly." They were all watery. The old smelly juice stains the fingers peeling the potato skin. The smell of these hands made people unhappy. But Mary was a good-tempered daughter. She could always endure the mill of the potatoes; because the colors, youth, and healthy atmosphere were rising in her whole body. When she finished peeling the potatoes and was free again, Anli couldn't bear it anymore. He hugged this daughter. She said: "Don't make jokes!"

Besides that, she didn't have anything else to say. She became silent. She had no more work to do. The time had come. Anli felt a faint sweetness on the corner of this daughter's lips, and saw a mole. At this time, the sound of the front door opening came. Fortunately, the door from the front door to the kitchen was closed. Mary whispered: "The master is back!"

There was no time to hesitate. But it was impossible to run away like this. Anli didn't know what crime it was to just run into someone's house. He accepted his fate even if it was a capital crime. Mary gave him a way to escape. He agreed without thinking.

In the corner of the kitchen, there was a dark room, about the size of a wooden cabinet, which was usually used to store dirty things. He had no choice but to run in there.

How many days did he stay inside? It took him a long time to realize that he had only stayed for a little over an hour. After a while, Mary came to call him, saying that Mr. Li Chai had left the house. Now, he could do whatever he wanted, but he only wanted to run away. He walked past this daughter and looked at her. Her eyes were big and dull. It made people feel that no matter how long they looked into her eyes, they would not find any expression. She looked so stupid. Even if she had beautiful cheeks, people would not notice them. She was fat and had small wrinkles, and her fingers looked swollen. There were many potatoes like her. She and the cow were only different in form. She smelled of domestic animals.
