Heilongjiang Men's Basketball Team (Photo by Wang Kai)

The Organizing Committee of the Games Discusses and Corrects Order Overnight; Fourteen Measures Resolved on the Spot 240

The order at the opening ceremony of the Games was extremely chaotic. Therefore, Organizing Committee member Wang Zhengting convened an emergency meeting that evening at the Lizhi Society, gathering all Organizing Committee members, heads of various departments, director-generals, deputy director-generals, chief referees, and deputy chief referees to discuss important issues such as strictly correcting order at the venue, transportation, and publicity. The meeting lasted until around 2:00 AM this morning. The details of the resolved items are as follows: (1) Four military police officers will be stationed at each stand to maintain order: sitting is permitted, but standing and crossing the stands are not. The security team is responsible for enforcement. (2) Spectators are absolutely prohibited from running on the athletic field. The security team and scouts are responsible for enforcement. (3) Only two people from each team (the team leader and deputy leader) and two staff members, six people from the venue team, and doctors, nurses, and stretcher bearers will be allowed to pass through the athletic field for important matters. They will be issued special red badges and allowed to pass in the reserved lane and in front of the command platform. (4) A signpost will be erected every five feet to guide spectators. (5) Ten scouts will be stationed at the east and west command platforms to communicate information. (6) Team representatives, instructors, managers, and athletes from each unit are not allowed to enter the athletic field. Athletes must register at the athlete registration area before each event and be led into the venue by the referee. (7) The area south of the west command platform, designated by a "Z" shaped platform, is entirely reserved for news reporters, clearly marked with large characters. Military police will be stationed to strictly guard it. Only those with news reporter identification cards are allowed to enter. (9) Athletes are prohibited from climbing randomly on the railings inside the athletic field. (10) Vendors are not allowed to enter the athletic field and stands. (11) Spectators must have the small corner of their ticket torn off by the ticket collector to be allowed to enter and exit the venue. (12) Ten police officers will be stationed at the basketball court, forty police officers at the soccer field, and four police officers at the swimming pool to maintain order. (13) Rickshaws must travel on one side of the road in a straight line and are not allowed to travel two abreast. (14) The direction of traffic has been changed. From the city to the venue, vehicles will exit Zhongshan Gate, take the asphalt road, pass the Mausoleum, and arrive at the sports field.

Shanghai Swimmer Wen Jingling to Depart for Beijing Today 241

Shanghai swimmer Wen Jingling will depart for Beijing today. Because the swimming competition at the National Games will not begin until the 16th and classes at Shanghai University are very strict, Wen Jingling has remained at the school for practice in recent days. Since the school has a swimming pool, remaining at the school for practice is not much different from going to Beijing for training. Wen Jingling plans to depart on the morning train of the 13th with Peng Sanmei to participate in the National Games.

Shanghai's Gu Yu, a Heroic Son and Daughter 242

Gu Yu, the man from Shanghai who broke the national high jump record, is short and stout, and a native of Jiading, Jiangsu. He is 22 years old. He currently serves as the Director of Promotion at the Dahua Sports Equipment Company in Shanghai and the Guangdong Brothers Tree Company. He graduated from Shanghai Minli Middle School and studied education at Datong University for one year. Due to economic difficulties, he had to drop out midway and enter the world. His father worked in the transportation industry, and he deeply disapproved of Yu's sports pursuits. Later, Yu won a school championship, which greatly pleased his mother. Therefore, Yu worked harder, practicing the 100-meter dash, 100-meter hurdles, triple jump, and long jump. While in Shanghai, he received guidance from Mr. Sun Duogu, which further improved his skills. At the first National Games held in Hangzhou, at the age of 19, he finished fifth in the high jump. This time, he unexpectedly succeeded, all thanks to Mr. Sun's guidance and his own diligent practice. This time, his result was 1.81 meters, higher than his usual practice result, more than a foot above his head. In the future, he plans to study Japanese to prepare for studying in Japan, etc.

Miss Li Yuanfen 243

The Guangdong female athlete, Li Yuanfen, broke the national long jump record yesterday. Her resume is of great concern to most observers. Miss Li is from Taishan County, Guangdong Province. Due to the large number of overseas Chinese in that county, she was exposed to and influenced by a progressive atmosphere from a young age, paying great attention to sports and possessing a natural talent for it. She began to show her talent when she was at the Guangzhou Municipal Normal School. At that time, the first National Games were held in Hangzhou. Miss Li was qualified to represent the school, but due to delays, we are only able to witness her heroic appearance today. Miss Li is currently a second-year student at the National Sun Yat-sen University High School. In March of this year, at the South China Four University Joint Sports Meet, she won the women's championship. She has exceptional achievements in various sports. When practicing the long jump, she exceeded five meters. However, due to the influence of the wind during yesterday's competition, the result was slightly reduced, but it still broke the national record. She has recorded 13.8 seconds in the 100-meter dash, reached 1.33 meters in the high jump, and over nine meters in the triple jump. Throwing a softball is also a specialty of Miss Li. At the first Guangdong track and field competition, she won first place with a score of 42 meters. This time, she is participating in the National Games, but due to regulatory constraints, she only registered for four events: the 50-meter dash, 100-meter dash, 400-meter relay, and long jump, which failed to fully demonstrate her talent. Miss Li also has expertise in academics and enjoys music. When reporters visited her, she was playing the harmonica and singing, with fluctuating rhythms and profound emotion, leaving a lingering and unforgettable impression. She is 18 years old this year, young and promising, with many talents and skills. It is hoped that she will work hard to create new records in various fields and bring glory to the country.

Observations from the Sidelines Yesterday: The Flowers of Hong Kong are Surrounded Everywhere 244

Among the female athletes' outfits, the Hong Kong team's was the most distinctive, with rose-colored wool upper garments and patterned silk pants for sports, making them look like fairies. The most beautiful faces belonged to the famous swimming sisters, Yang Xiuqiong and Yang Xiushan, whose figures were also graceful and slender. Wherever the beautiful horses went, they were surrounded by crowds. The temporary shops and restaurants were crowded at mealtimes. For a time it was felt that the flowers of Hong Kong were a bit over the top, which caused the Yang sisters some distress.

The Order of the Games is Gradually Improving 245

On the second day of the Games, the weather was overcast, and the number of spectators decreased by six or seven tenths. Traffic was no longer obstructed, and the order of the venue was gradually improving. Only a few thousand people dotted the stands of the athletic field. News reporters could also access the east command platform, and the radio broadcast of results was also very clear. It can be said that things are gradually improving.

Wang Zhengting Praises Liu Changchun 246

Wang Zhengting, a member of the Organizing Committee of the Games, arrived at the venue at 9:30 AM with his wife, Miss Smillie, and took a high seat on the west command platform. He carried a program, listened to reports, and recorded them in the program at any time, repeatedly saying that the results were not bad and that he was very interested. When Liu Changchun appeared in the third group during the 100-meter semi-finals, there was a burst of applause. As the starting gun fired, he ran like the wind. Cheng Jinguan initially took the lead, but after 30 meters, Liu intensified his pace. Cheng initially gritted his teeth and tried to compete, but after 50 meters, he could not sustain his strength and gradually fell behind. By the time he reached the finish line, Liu had left Cheng five or six meters behind. Mr. and Mrs. Wang clapped their hands loudly, repeatedly saying that the veteran was impressive and rare. When they heard that the result was 10.7 seconds, they praised him even more.
